# Welcome | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

![Page cover](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252F5SGqWTmDgWH2Tv9mODRT%252FMotorbikes.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8580526-7341-449d-b189-5158f933adb5&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c31e5df&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/#rust-console-edition-community-server-wiki)

**Rust Console Edition Community Server Wiki**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This comprehensive resource serves as a guide to setting up, managing, and customising your Rust Console Edition community server. Whether you are an experienced server administrator or brand new to custom servers, this wiki aims to equip you with the knowledge to create and manage your ideal Rust Console Edition experience.

circle-info

Find out more here! [https://rust.double11.com/community-serversarrow-up-right](https://rust.double11.com/community-servers)

circle-info

Create a server!

GPORTAL: [https://www.g-portal.com/en/gameserver/rust-server-hosting-psarrow-up-right](https://www.g-portal.com/en/gameserver/rust-server-hosting-ps)
 NITRADO: [https://server.nitrado.net/en-GBarrow-up-right](https://server.nitrado.net/en-GB)

View the [Server Setup](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/server-setup)
 page for a quick start or visit [Configuring a Server](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/configuring-a-server)
 for a more detailed look at server management.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/#server-setup-and-configuration)

**Server Setup and Configuration**

*   **Establish your server**
    
    *   Step-by-step instructions on creating and setting up your Rust Console Edition community server. [Getting started](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/server-setup)
        
    
*   **Fine-tune server parameters**
    
    *   Gain expertise in customising essential server settings to align with your gameplay preferences. [Configuring a Server](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/configuring-a-server)
        
    
*   **Explore map presets**
    
    *   Identify and select the appropriate map options for your Rust Console Edition community server. [Map Presets](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-presets)
         [Map Settings](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings)
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/#server-management-and-maintenance)

**Server Management and Maintenance**

*   **Secure your server with admin roles**
    
    *   Assign appropriate admin privileges to maintain server integrity and enforce community guidelines. [Permissions](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/permissions)
        
    
*   **Service and back up your server**
    
    *   Implement regular server restarts to ensure optimal performance and stability. Implement regular server backups to safeguard data against potential loss. [Restarts and Backup](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup)
        
    
*   **Logs and management**
    
    *   Utilise server tools to change settings, view game & server logs and more. [Logs, Booting & Saving](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/logs-booting-and-saving)
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/#console-and-in-game-commands)

**Console and In-game Commands**

*   **Administer your server with console commands**
    
    *   Master a comprehensive range of console commands to control and customise your server's operation. [Commands](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/gameplay)
        
    
*   **Engage in-game interactions**
    
    *   Leverage in-game commands to enhance gameplay experiences with tools like: [Event Settings](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings)
        
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/#community-guidelines-and-communications)

**Community Guidelines and Communications**

*   **Uphold community standards**
    
    *   Give players role and permissions to help create the server community you want. [Authority Levels & Privileges](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges)
        
    
*   **Seek community support**
    
    *   Utilise in game chat and broadcast to speak to players, and set messages to make players feel welcome. [Moderation Actions](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions)
        
    

[NextServer Setupchevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/server-setup)

# General Warnings | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

Here is a list of some general warnings that will help you when using your custom server:

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/general-warnings#saving-changes-reboots-your-server)

Saving changes reboots your server


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

Keep in mind that a "Save Changes" button will appear if you change anything on these pages, so hold off until you have made all of your intended changes, or the server will reboot before you are finished customising!

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/general-warnings#make-sure-you-set-yourself-as-owner)

Make sure you set yourself as Owner


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-check

In order to have control of your server in-game, you must first assign your GamerTag \[XBOX\] or PSN ID \[PlayStation\] to be an Owner in the Boot Commands. (see [Configuring a Server](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/configuring-a-server)
)

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/general-warnings#avoid-bad-performance)

Avoid bad performance


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

Please keep in mind that spawning excessive amounts of items on the server can lead to server lag, crashes, client instability, and general misery due to console hardware limitations.

circle-exclamation

It is strongly recommended to set a regular wipe schedule!

triangle-exclamation

Servers without a scheduled wipe every month (at least) will be prone to instability, client/server crashes, and general misery.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/general-warnings#back-up-your-servers)

Back up your servers


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

It is strongly recommended to create regular backups of your server! [Back up your servers](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/general-warnings#back-up-your-servers)

circle-exclamation

When booting a server, please wait for 10-15 minutes as the server works silently at some points. This may look like the server is frozen, but it’s not!

triangle-exclamation

Servers without automatic backups can lead to loss of progress, client instability, and general misery.

[PreviousStatus Pagechevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/status-page)
[NextPermissionschevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/permissions)

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Saving changes reboots your server](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/general-warnings#saving-changes-reboots-your-server)
    
*   [Make sure you set yourself as Owner](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/general-warnings#make-sure-you-set-yourself-as-owner)
    
*   [Avoid bad performance](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/general-warnings#avoid-bad-performance)

# Permissions | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

The permissions page provides owners with a way to add other people to help with server creation, administration and customisation.

If you are the one who has purchased the server, you will be able to access the server settings etc. by default.

circle-exclamation

NITRADO currently does not have this functionality, but stay tuned as we work on updates!

For other users, you will need to add their GPORTAL username into this input field, so that they can access the server also.

This option does not have any effect on the in-game permissions, and is solely for providing access to the GPORTAL page itself.

1.  Visit the [GPORTAL websitearrow-up-right](https://www.g-portal.com/en)
    .
    
2.  Click on the **\[Permissions\]** tab on the left side of the screen.
    
3.  Type GPORTAL username of the user you wish to add.
    
4.  Click add user.
    

[PreviousGeneral Warningschevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/general-warnings)
[NextConfiguring a Serverchevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/configuring-a-server)

# Status Page | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

Once you rent a server from, you will be presented with the following screens, depending on who your provider is:

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FbycP7PDaXdXmtA2hIviM%252FRust.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddcc58575-8396-4173-b985-953843fd6882&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3083c0b9&sv=2)

The GPORTAL Status Page

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252F6tNS8M2Toxg6bMU9fRZV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9305c113-fae9-4b42-8f2b-33bb68254062&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b12cc1ea&sv=2)

The NITRADO Status Page (Dashboard)

This is the status page, used for tracking the health and basic information about your newly created server.

Each server is assigned a dedicated amount of CPU usage and RAM storage. This usually won’t be an issue, but this area can be useful for monitoring your server’s health if you are worried about things getting out of hand.

If you notice that your server is running slowly, or experiencing lag/disconnects, consider lowering some settings, disabling some custom commands, or wiping the server. All of these options are customisable in the GPORTAL | NITRADO options page, and a guide on how to do this is displayed in the following sections.

Before you boot your server up for the first time, let’s walk through all of the settings that you can customise your server with!

[PreviousServer Setupchevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/server-setup)
[NextGeneral Warningschevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/general-warnings)

Last updated 8 months ago

# Server Setup | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

1.  Go to the main [GPORTALarrow-up-right](https://www.g-portal.com/en)
     | [NITRADOarrow-up-right](https://server.nitrado.net/en-GB)
     page.
    
2.  Go to **\[My Servers\] | \[My Services\]** where you should be able to access all of your rented servers.
    
3.  After selecting your server, you can change many options, but for now let’s stick to the basics:
    
    *   Name
        
    *   Password
        
    *   Map
        
    *   Seed
        
    *   Player Count
        
    *   Map Size
        
    *   Monuments
        
    

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/server-setup#to-set-yourself-as-an-owner)

To set yourself as an Owner


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to **\[Console\]** over on the left on the GPORTAL | NITRADO website and type the following command:

Copy

    OwnerID "Your Gamertag/PSN ID"

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/server-setup#to-add-other-tiers)

To add other tiers


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    AdminID "Gamertag/PSN ID"
    ModeratorID "Gamertag/PSN ID"
    VIPID "Gamertag/PSN ID"

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/server-setup#to-revoke-tier-rights)

To revoke tier rights


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[PreviousWelcomechevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers)
[NextStatus Pagechevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/getting-started/status-page)

Copy

    RemoveAdmin "Gamertag/PSN ID"
    RemoveModerator "Gamertag/PSN ID"
    RemoveVIP "Gamertag/PSN ID"

# Map Presets | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

In this section, you are presented with a selection of maps that have been hand-picked by the Double Eleven team. You are free to choose one of these “presets”, and the map will generate once you click the associated map image.

All maps will attempt to spawn all monuments by default, but you can edit this to get the monuments you want.

![GPORTAL Preset Menu](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.squarespace-cdn.com%2Fcontent%2Fv1%2F602d246245658135031e4b2a%2F5c537d47-4ccf-47f4-afd9-a84911d2fd6d%2FCleanShot%2B2023-11-29%2Bat%2B15.44.12%25402x.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56a0c789&sv=2)

GPORTAL Preset Menu

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FTUKTkczJPte0LDP11j0x%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D157a73aa-006f-47fd-8bc8-09cf24bc033f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a91d4888&sv=2)

NITRADO Preset Menu

circle-info

When you select a preset, the server will prompt you asking if you are sure you want to generate a new map. This step is usually best saved for last, as it will **automatically restart** once you choose a new map.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.squarespace-cdn.com%2Fcontent%2Fv1%2F602d246245658135031e4b2a%2Fd3dc6f0f-67f1-4de3-99c6-012a1df88037%2FCleanShot%2B2023-11-29%2Bat%2B15.40.54%25402x.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2779fb4&sv=2)

# Custom Boot Commands | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

In this section, you can add [server commandsarrow-up-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#enable-whitelist)
 which will run every time the server boots. There are multiple features that can run on boot, which are listed below.

You can enter any combination of these commands, and examples & formatting guides will be provided along the way. You can add more than more one command in the settings box, separated on new lines.

* * *

circle-exclamation

_**Keep in mind that settings in the boot commands will require the server to reboot.**_

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/custom-boot-commands#example-boot-command-entry)

**Example boot command entry**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    OwnerID "XxXL337HaX0rXxX"
    ModeratorID "ModOfHellfire"
    global.whitelistid "PlayerOne"
    global.whitelistid "PlayerTwo"
    banitem "rifle.ak" "NoBlueprintSpawn NoTechTree"
    setmodifier "hatchet" "tool" "2"
    furnaceusagemultiplier "2"
    monumentspawns.enableconfig "stables_recycler"
    monumentspawns.enableconfig "cargoship_recycler"

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/custom-boot-commands#effects-of-the-commands-above)

**Effects of the commands above:**

*   A player with the gamertag _**XxXL337HaX0rXxX**_ is set as the Owner of the server and has [Ownerarrow-up-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges#tier-4-owner)
     privileges (highlighted red).
    
*   A player gamertag _**ModOfHellfire**_ is set to be a Moderator in the server, and can access [Moderator-tierarrow-up-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/moderation)
     options (highlighted blue).
    
*   Players with the gamertags _**PlayerOne**_ and _**PlayerTwo**_ are on the [Whitelistarrow-up-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#enable-whitelist)
    .
    
*   The Assault Rifle blueprint can’t spawn and the Assault Rifle can’t be found in the Tech Tree.
    
*   The Hatchet will now have 2x gather rate.
    
*   The Furnace will now burn twice as much fuel as normal.
    
*   Recyclers will now spawn at the Large Barn and the Cargo Ship.
    

[PreviousBasic Settingschevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings)
[NextMap Presetschevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-presets)

Last updated 5 months ago

# 💥OLD GEN ONLY💥 Donut Island Setup | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

For server owner on GPORTAL, a new map preset has been introduced with the latest update!

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-presets/old-gen-only-donut-island-setup#preset)

Preset


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you start, check if you have a preset applied already. You can find this out if one of the preset icons is outlined, as such:

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252Fpit0bMZQSyCfMqdFWKjR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6393dfe-b2c1-4d13-8604-cd909c65ae8a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80ad96df&sv=2)

If this is the case, you should follow these steps:

1.  Execute a **FULL WIPE** of your server using the button on the "Status" page of your server.
    

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252F99o05qekSId4aTYHOMip%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D414a6c52-2e9c-4744-b492-bcd118a0540c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7697bf85&sv=2)

1.  Load into the server once it has rebooted, and make sure it executes a **SAVE**.
    
2.  Execute another **FULL WIPE** of your server using the button on the "Status" page of your server.
    
3.  Wait for the server to execute the full wipe. You may need to re-edit some settings in your server configuration.
    
4.  Select the Donut Island preset:
    

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FaZ3TzdNev2ChfcTKDgS2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7fde6433-b1e5-41a7-a4f7-e69afe3264be&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6fc66ce&sv=2)

1.  Wait for your server to boot
    
2.  Enjoy the Donut Island!
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-presets/old-gen-only-donut-island-setup#no-preset)

No Preset


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you do **not** have a preset, you should follow these steps instead:

1.  Choose any random preset from the options, excluding Donut Island:
    

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252Fl3D0N9XqDM9Ce6kY4dDT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba80c39f-4f86-4dd3-b0e8-e0b018038a16&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3a830aba&sv=2)

1.  Load into the server once it has booted, and make sure it executes a **SAVE**.
    

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FwURV70KRXLP0rB5O7M7Q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De0dbbc36-3e39-4d00-90fa-4c3b4c08fd2d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f5f44d9e&sv=2)

1.  Execute another **FULL WIPE** of your server using the button on the "Status" page of your server.
    
2.  Wait for the server to execute the full wipe. You may need to re-edit some settings in your server configuration.
    
3.  Select the Donut Island preset:
    
4.  ![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FaZ3TzdNev2ChfcTKDgS2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7fde6433-b1e5-41a7-a4f7-e69afe3264be&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6fc66ce&sv=2)
    
5.  Wait for your server to boot
    
6.  Enjoy the Donut Island!

# Configuring a Server | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

This page assumes you have already purchased a server and have followed the steps in the getting started guide.

triangle-exclamation

Keep in mind that a “Save Changes” button will appear if you change anything on the server pages. While it is good practise to save often, we recommend that you hold off until you have made all of your intended changes, otherwise the server will reboot before you are finished customising

The structure of this section mimics the structure of the server settings section. You get to it by pressing the button labelled 1 in the screenshot, and can jump to the correct sections using tab links labelled 2. A guide to each of these can be accessed using the menu below.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FqYm3yuRA2yzPfLbdlN7I%252FServer%2520Configuration.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db95eb1d8-ad40-4cd8-8c5b-d7c0372d383b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4b6f83e3&sv=2)

GPORTAL Settings Interface

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252Ftzth5St4Y5D3tIEGQ3wY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D813b1fbb-ad4c-4882-8df7-cda3bb66bd2b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7cdbfd1b&sv=2)

NITRADO Settings Interface

* * *

circle-info

_**Commands and features marked with a**_ **👢** _**symbol must be run in the Custom Boot Commands section of GPORTAL | NITRADO.**_

circle-info

_**Commands and functions marked with a**_ **📟** _**must be entered in the GPORTAL | NITRADO Console. Commands marked with this symbol are also available to run in-game.**_

_**Exclusive in-game commands are noted below.**_

circle-info

_**Commands marked with a**_ **🎮** _**must be entered in the In-Game Console, in the Control Panel.**_

circle-info

_**Commands marked with**_ **💥** _**currently do not function as intended. This status will be updated as fixes come out.**_

circle-info

_**When restarting, some of the commands that you enter into the console may be overridden by the settings in the GPORTAL | NITRADO Page.**_

_**These commands will be marked with a**_ **🌌**_**.**_

# World Settings | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

This section of option controls how the world works in-game. This is especially useful for special server types like PvE, as they can be combined with other sections to create the perfect server type.

Here, you can customise the following settings to your liking, below are all the options and a summary of each one.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#quick-reference)

Quick reference


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Option

Description

RHIB Population

Controls the amount of RHIBs that spawn naturally on the coastline.

Rowboat Population

Controls the amount of rowboats that spawn naturally on the coastline.

Rowboat Decay Time (Outside)

Controls the time taken for a rowboat to despawn when it is near the coastline.

Rowboat Decay Time (Deep Water)

Controls the time taken for a rowboat to despawn when it is **not** near the coastline.

Rowboat Decay Time (Start Time)

Controls the time taken for a rowboat to decay once it has not been interacted with.

Stability

Toggles the stability of player-made structures, allowing players to create wacky structures.

Radiation

Toggles the radiation of certain monuments on the map.

Time Progression

Toggles the progression of time on the server.

Day Length

Sets the length of the day time, in real-world minutes.

Night Length

Sets the length of the night time, in real-world minutes.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#rhib-population)

RHIB Population


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the amount of RHIBs that spawn naturally on the coastline.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#input)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 20 (per km²).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#notes)

**Notes**

Default is 0 per km².

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#restart-required)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#rowboat-population)

Rowboat Population


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the amount of rowboats that spawn naturally on the coastline.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#input-1)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 20 (per km²).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#notes-1)

**Notes**

Default is 4 per km².

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#restart-required-1)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#rowboat-decay-time-outside)

Rowboat Decay Time (Outside)


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the time taken for a rowboat to despawn when it is near the coastline.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#input-2)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² minutes. (Essentially infinite)

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#notes-2)

**Notes**

Time is measured in real-world minutes.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#restart-required-2)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#rowboat-decay-time-deep-water)

Rowboat Decay Time (Deep Water)


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the time taken for a rowboat to despawn when it is **not** near the coastline.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#input-3)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² minutes. (Essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#notes-3)

**Notes**

Time is meaured in real-world minutes.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#restart-required-3)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#rowboat-decay-time-start-time)

Rowboat Decay Time (Start Time)


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the time taken for a rowboat to decay once it has not been interacted with.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#input-4)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² seconds. (Essentially infinite)

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#notes-4)

**Notes**

Time is measure in real-world seconds.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#restart-required-4)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#stability)

Stability


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles the stability of player-made structures, allowing players to create wacky structures.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#input-5)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default ON.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#notes-5)

**Notes**

Disabling this can be useful for PvE Servers and build-test servers.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#restart-required-5)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#radiation)

Radiation


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles the radiation of certain monuments on the map.

####

**Input**

Toggle-able, default ON.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#notes-6)

**Notes**

Disabling this can be useful for PvE Servers and build-test servers.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#restart-required-6)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

####

Toggle-able, default ON.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#notes-7)

Disabling this can be useful for PvE Servers and build-test servers.

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

Day Length


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sets the length of the day time, in real-world minutes.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#input-8)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 1440 minutes.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#notes-8)

**Notes**

For eternal daytime, consider disabling Time Progression instead of setting this value.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings#restart-required-8)

Yes

For eternal nighttime, consider disabling Time Progression instead of setting this value.

# Map Settings | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

For more advanced customisation of the map, this section contains multiple options for full control over the creation of your map.

These options will require a full restart of the server, as the map has to generate from scratch every time a change is made. Map settings are best saved for last.

Here, you can customise the following settings to your liking, below are all the options and a summary of each one.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#quick-reference)

Quick reference


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

triangle-exclamation

Changes to any settings that affect map generation will always require a server restart.

Option

Description

Seed

Determines the seed that your server will use for procedural map generation.

Max Players

Determines the maximum amount of players that can be connected to the server simultaneously. Additional players will be added to the server queue upon connection.

World Size

Determines the size of a server based on the length of one of its sides.

Land Monuments

Determines the monuments that will attempt to spawn on the server. Monument spawning is not guaranteed, and locations & populations of monuments will vary from seed to seed. Junkyard and Raidable base will not spawn, even if selected.

Offshore Monuments

Determines the monuments that will spawn on the server. Offshore Monument spawning is guaranteed, and will spawn every time, as they are not affected by random map generation.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#seed)

Seed


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Determines the seed that your server will use for procedural map generation.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#notes)

**Notes**

This can be any whole number, and every map will be different, depending on the seed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#restart-required)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#max-players)

Max Players


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Determines the maximum amount of players that can be connected to the server simultaneously. Additional players will be added to the server queue upon connection.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#notes-1)

**Notes**

For now, we have limited this to 1→100.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#restart-required-1)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#world-size)

World Size


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Determines the size of a server based on the length of one of its sides.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#notes-2)

**Notes**

For example, a 3.5k server is a server with approximate size of 12.25km² (3.5k×3.5k).

For now, this is limited to 1km→3.5km, in intervals of 0.5k.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#restart-required-2)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#land-monuments)

Land Monuments


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Determines the monuments that will **attempt** to spawn on the server.

Monument spawning is not guaranteed, and locations & populations of monuments will vary from seed to seed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#notes-3)

**Notes**

Most pre-made maps will have all monuments, but it may require a few tries to get the monuments you want by choosing from the list.

Feel free to disable any monuments you don’t want, as this will increase the chance of preferred monuments spawning.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#restart-required-3)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#offshore-monuments)

Offshore Monuments


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Determines the monuments that will spawn on the server.

Offshore Monument spawning **is** guaranteed, as they are not affected by random map generation.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#notes-4)

**Notes**

There can be a maximum of 2 Oil Rigs and 2 Cargo Ships per server, placed randomly in the ocean surrounding the island.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-settings#restart-required-4)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

[Previous💥OLD GEN ONLY💥 Donut Island Setupchevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/map-presets/old-gen-only-donut-island-setup)
[NextWorld Settingschevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/world-settings)

Last updated 6 months ago

# NPC Settings | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

This section controls the spawning, behaviour and population of NPCs, Animals, and Scientists around the map. As of right now, monument Scientists cannot be disabled and are always active.

Here, you can customise the following settings to your liking, below are all the options and a summary of each one.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#quick-reference)

Quick reference


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Option

Description

AI Thinking

Toggles AI thinking, essentially controlling the function of AI NPCs as a whole. This command controls AI shooting/movement/detection/pathfinding, and will supercede the other AI toggles.

AI Movement

Toggles AI movement, controlling the movement of NPCs.

AI Player Detection

Toggles AI targeting of players.

NPC Junkpile Spawn Chance

Controls the chance that a Junkpile Scientist will spawn on any junkpile on the map.

Bear Population

Controls the density of bear spawning per km².

Boar Population

Controls the density of boar spawning per km².

Chicken Population

Controls the density of chicken spawning per km².

Deer Population

Controls the density of deer spawning per km².

Rideable Horse Population

Controls the density of horse spawning per km².

Wolf Population

Controls the density of wolf spawning per km².

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#ai-thinking)

AI Thinking


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles AI thinking, essentially controlling the function of AI NPCs as a whole.

This command controls AI shooting/movement/detection/pathfinding, and will supercede the other AI toggles.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#input)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default ON.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#notes)

**Notes**

Disabling this can be useful for PvE Servers and build-test servers. If this is off, the other AI toggles will have no effect.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#restart-required)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#ai-movement)

AI Movement


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles AI movement, controlling the movement of NPCs.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#input-1)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default ON.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#notes-1)

**Notes**

Disabling this can be useful for PvE Servers and build-test servers.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#restart-required-1)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#ai-player-detection)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#input-2)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default ON.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#notes-2)

**Notes**

Disabling this can be useful for PvE Servers and build-test servers.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#restart-required-2)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#npc-junkpile-spawn-chance)

NPC Junkpile Spawn Chance


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the chance that a Junkpile Scientist will spawn on any junkpile on the map.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#input-3)

**Input**

Any number, but this number is clamped to 100.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#notes-3)

**Notes**

Setting this to maximum will guarantee that a Scientist spawns on every Junkpile available.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#restart-required-3)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#bear-population)

Bear Population


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the density of bear spawning per km².

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#input-4)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 20 (per km²).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#notes-4)

**Notes**

For example, setting this to 10 would result in 10 bears per km².

On a 3K map, this would be: 10 × 3k × 3k = 90 bears on the whole map.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#restart-required-4)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#boar-population)

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/npc-settings#notes-5)

# Basic Settings | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

On the basic settings page, you will be presented with a long list of options from which you can customise your server. This can be overwhelming for new owners at first, so let’s review the settings which are available to you, section-by-section:

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#quick-reference)

Quick reference


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Option

Description

Name

This controls the name of your server, and what will appear on the in-game server list.

Password

This determines a password for the server, which players will need to enter before joining.

Platform

You can make a server accessible to all players (Crossplay) , or restrict it to players on a specific console platform.

Welcome Message

Welcome message to greet players when they join the server. Admins will also receive this message. Accepts regular text, adhering to profanity guidelines.

First-Time Join Message

Message sent to all players when a player joins for the first time.

Just Joined Message

Message sent to all players when a player joins every time they enter the server. Accepts regular text, adhering to profanity guidelines.

Left Message

Message sent to all players when a player leaves the server.

Rage Quit Message

Message sent to all players when someone "Rage Quits". Rage-quitting is when a player leaving after dying in the game.

Admin Message

Message shown exclusively Admins when they join the server.

Admin Broadcast

This will turn on or turn off a broadcast message that appears in the chat box when Admins perform actions, such as activating NoClip, God Mode.

Welcome Screen

Toggles the Welcome Screen, a screen shown to all players when they join the server. Owners can customise this screen to show rules, messages, and active Admins/Moderators.

Welcome Screen Text

Message shown on the front page of the Welcome Screen when a player joins the server.

Server Rules Message

Message that shows on the "Rules" tab of the Welcome Screen.

Server Team Tab

Toggles whether the "Server Team" tab shows on the Welcome Screen. This shows active Owners/Admins/Moderators. If you would like your Admin team to remain anonymous, this can be safely switched off.

Server Rules Tab

Toggles whether the "Rules" tab shows on the Welcome Screen. Owners can create their own rules for the server and players must agree to them if they want to play on your server.

Enable Whitelist

This toggle will enable the Whitelist function, allowing only Whitelisted players to join the server.

Player Report Cooldown

This option allows the owner to set the cooldown for multiple reports from other players. Once a user has submitted a report, they will not be able to create another until the cooldown has expired.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#name)

Name


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This controls the name of your server, and what will appear on the in-game server list.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#input)

Input

Any name you like, as long as it adheres to profanity guidelines.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#notes)

**Notes**

While it will appear as a valid entry on GPORTAL | NITRADO, players on console won’t be able to see your server name in game if it gets censored. Characters will be replaced by \* - so make sure to keep it clean!

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#restart-required)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#server-colours)

Server Colours

Users can edit the text colour of their server name, which is useful for making your server stand out in the list.

You can change the colour of your server name by entering the following information into the "Name" box of the GPORTAL | NITRADO Server Settings area.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#password)

Password


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This determines a password for the server, which players will need to enter before joining.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#input-1)

Input

Any password you like, as long as it adheres to profanity guidelines. Keep this empty for no password.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#notes-1)

**Notes**

While it will appear as a valid entry on GPORTAL | NITRADO, players on console won’t be able to use this password if it gets censored, so make sure to keep it clean!

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#restart-required-1)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#platform)

Platform


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can make a server accessible to all players (Crossplay) or restrict it to players on a specific console platform.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#input-2)

Input

There are 3 Options: Xbox Only / PlayStation / Crossplay

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#notes-2)

**Notes**

Crossplay is visible to all player. Servers set to a specific platform will be invisible to players on other platforms.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#restart-required-2)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#welcome-message)

Welcome Message


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Welcome message to greet players when they join the server. Admins will also receive this message. Accepts regular text, adhering to profanity guidelines.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#input-3)

Input

Accepts regular text, adhering to profanity guidelines. Has a character limit. Leave blank for no message.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#notes-3)

**Notes**

In-game, the message will read: \[Player Name\] \[Welcome Message\] - entering "Welcome to the server!" for a message that reads: "Player Name - Welcome to the server!"

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#restart-required-3)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#first-time-join-message)

First-Time Join Message


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Message sent to all players when a player joins for the first time.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#input-4)

Input

Accepts regular text, adhering to profanity guidelines. Has a character limit. Leave blank for no message.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#notes-4)

**Notes**

In-game, the message will read: \[Player Name\] \[First-Time Join Message\]. This can be useful to enter something like "has just discovered the server!" for a message that reads: "Player Name has just discovered the server!"

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#restart-required-4)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#just-joined-message)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Message sent to all players when a player joins for the first time.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#input-5)

Input

Accepts regular text, adhering to profanity guidelines. Has a character limit. Leave blank for no message.

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Message sent to all players when a player leaves the server.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#input-6)

Input

Accepts regular text, adhering to profanity guidelines. Has a character limit. Leave blank for no message.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#notes-6)

**Notes**

In-game, the message will read: \[Player Name\] \[Left Message\]. It can be useful to enter something like "has left the server!" for a message that reads: "PlayerName has left the server!"

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#restart-required-6)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#rage-quit-message)

Rage Quit Message


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Message sent to all players when someone "Rage Quits". Rage-quitting is when a player leaving after dying in the game.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#input-7)

Input

Accepts regular text, adhering to profanity guidelines. Has a character limit. Leave blank for no message.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#notes-7)

**Notes**

In-game, the message will read: \[Player Name\] \[Rage Quit Message\]. It can be useful to enter something like "has just rage-quit the server!" for a message that reads: "PlayerName has just rage-quit the server!"

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#restart-required-7)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#admin-message)

Admin Message


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Message shown exclusively Admins when they join the server.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#input-8)

Input

ON / OFF - this is OFF by default

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#notes-8)

**Notes**

You can set the list of Whitelisted players in the Custom Boot Commands section. There is also a Whitelisted players list in-game, for viewing only, managing the list is only available on the G-Portal website.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#restart-required-8)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#admin-broadcast)

Admin Broadcast


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This will turn on or turn of a broadcast message that appear in the chat box when Admins perform actions, such as activating NoClip, God Mode.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#input-9)

Input

ON / OFF - this is ON by default

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#restart-required-9)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#enable-whitelist)

Enable Whitelist


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This toggle will enable the Whitelist function, allowing only Whitelisted players to join the server.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#input-10)

Input

Accepts regular text, adhering to profanity guidelines. Has a character limit. Leave blank for no message.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#notes-9)

**Notes**

In-game, the message will read: \[Player Name\] \[Admin Message\]. It can be useful to enter something like "has just joined the server as an Admin!" for a message that reads: "Player Name has just joined the server as an Admin!"

A guide on how to set up Owner/Admin/Moderator/VIP privileges is [**here**arrow-up-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges)
.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#restart-required-10)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#player-report-cooldown)

Player Report Cooldown


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This option allows the owner to set the cooldown for multiple reports from other players. Once a user has submitted a report, they will not be able to create another until the cooldown has expired.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#input-11)

Input

Any number, the default is 5. Numbers represent real world minutes.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#notes-10)

**Notes**

You can set this to 0 for no cooldown, but beware of spam reports and potential instability.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/basic-settings#restart-required-11)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

# Custom Auth Levels | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

Server owners can now set custom authority tiers for convars in their server, by using the following commands:

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges/custom-auth-levels#undefined)
> 
> **📟🌌**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges/custom-auth-levels#setconvarauthlevel-command-tier)
> 
> _**setconvarauthlevel "command" "tier"**_
> 
> Where "command" is any command that you have access to, at owner level or lower,
> 
> and "tier" is the Auth Tier that you would like to set the command to.

The available Auth Tiers are as follows:

*   User
    
*   VIP
    
*   Moderator
    
*   Administrator
    
*   Owner
    

From here, you can make any command available (from the lists in this wiki) to any Auth Tier.

This means the Moderators and Administrators in your server can have more (or less) power, depending on what commands you choose to give them.

You can also assign Owner Tier commands to your Admins/Mods if you like.

Currently, we only allow Moderators/Administrators to access the in-game command console.

To view you current Auth Tier setup, you can use the following command:

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges/custom-auth-levels#undefined-1)
> 
> **📟🌌**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges/custom-auth-levels#getconvarauthlevel-command)
> 
> _**getconvarauthlevel "command"**_
> 
> Where "command" is any command that you have changed with this system.

circle-exclamation

_**These changes will persist over restarts, but does not keep a log, so make sure to keep a note of any changes you have made to commands!**_

[PreviousAuthority Levels & Privilegeschevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges)
[NextGranting User Tierschevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/granting-user-tiers)

Last updated 6 months ago

# Configuration Backups | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

circle-exclamation

Currently, only NITRADO servers offer this option.

On NITRADO servers, you can save a previously created server profile by going to the Configuration Profiles tab on the left side of the web interface.

A configuration profile consists of the following elements:

*   Server Settings such as:
    
    *   Seed
        
    *   World Size
        
    *   Player Count
        
    *   Server Name
        
    *   Whitelist
        
    *   Custom Commands
        
    
*   Map Preset
    
*   RCON Password
    
*   Wipe Mode/Schedule
    

An automatic backup of this profile is made daily. You can also create one manually by pressing the button at the top of the screen. This will save all of your current settings but has no effect on the state of the server (buildings, player locations, BPs).

[PreviousRestarts and Backupchevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup)
[NextModeration Actionschevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions)

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

Was this helpful?

# Monument Recycler Configs | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

The following settings can control the addition of Recyclers to certain monuments. Owners can enter them in the GPORTAL | NITRADO boot commands section so that they are saved to the server when it starts up.

triangle-exclamation

**Changing these settings will require a server WIPE**.

The exception to this rule is adding recyclers to the Cargo Ship, in which case no restart is required, but a fresh Cargo Ship will need to spawn.

triangle-exclamation

Most monument recycler commands **MUST** be entered into the boot command section and will not work while the server is running.

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/monument-recycler-configs#undefined)
> 
> **👢**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/monument-recycler-configs#monumentspawns.enableconfig-monument)
> 
> _**monumentspawns.enableconfig "monument"**_
> 
> Where "monument" is one of the following options:

Command

Description

`"dome_recycler"`

Enables the spawning of recyclers at the Dome.

`"fishing_village_large_recycler"`

Enables the spawning of recyclers at the Large Fishing Village.

`"fishing_village_small_recycler"`

Enables the spawning of recyclers at the Small Fishing Villages.

`"oilrig_large_recycler"`

Enables the spawning of recyclers at the Large Oil Rig.

`"oilrig_small_recycler"`

Enables the spawning of recyclers at the Small Oil Rig.

`"stables_recycler"`

Enables the spawning of recyclers at the Stables (Large Barn) and Ranch.

`"cargoship_recycler"`

Enables the spawning of recyclers on the Cargo Ship (both variants).

circle-info

_**Cargo Ship Recyclers:**_ Using the `forcespawnconfig "cargoship_recycler"` command will onlt spawn a Recycler on the **currently spawned** Cargo Ship. This setting will not persist over multiple Cargo Ships. For permanently spawning a Recycler on Cargo Ships, you must use the boot command: `monumentspawns.enableconfig "cargoship_recycler"`

* * *

Players can also disable these configurations by entering the following command:

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/monument-recycler-configs#undefined-1)
> 
> **👢**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/monument-recycler-configs#monumentspawns.disableconfig-monument)
> 
> _**monumentspawns.disableconfig "monument"**_
> 
> Where "monument" is any of the above options.

For viewing a list of configurations, use the following:

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/monument-recycler-configs#undefined-2)
> 
> **👢**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/monument-recycler-configs#monumentspawns.getconfigs)
> 
> _monumentspawns.getconfigs_
> 
> Returns a list of available configs.

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/monument-recycler-configs#undefined-3)
> 
> **👢**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/monument-recycler-configs#monumentspawns.getenabledconfigs)
> 
> _monumentspawns.getenabledconfigs_
> 
> Returns a list of currently enabled configs.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/monument-recycler-configs#config-force-change)

Config Force Change


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To skip the rebooting process and immediately generate recyclers at monuments without the need for a wipe, use the following command.

It is slightly more unstable, but shouldn't cause too many issues:

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/monument-recycler-configs#undefined-4)
> 
> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/monument-recycler-configs#monumentspawns.forcespawnconfig-monument)
> 
> _monumentspawns.forcespawnconfig “monument”_
> 
> Where "monument" is any of the above options.

[PreviousModifierschevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers)
[NextSeasonal Eventschevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events)

Last updated 6 months ago

# Command Scheduling | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

The Scheduler is a system that allows you to schedule commands to be run at certain times automatically. It can only be used via the GPORTAL | NITRADO console.

triangle-exclamation

The following commands cannot be scheduled:

*   entity.spawn
    
*   inventory.givedrop
    
*   spawnitem
    

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/command-scheduling#setup)

Setup

To create a Scheduler action, you must start the command with `CreateAction ConVarSchedulerAction`

Then, there are several arguments you can adjust:

`StartTime EndTime RepeatTime RepeatAmount Command CommandParams`

> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/command-scheduling#createaction-convarscheduleraction-0-1-2-3-4-5)
> 
> _CreateAction ConvarSchedulerAction_ `_[0] [1] [2] [3] [4] [5]_`
> 
> This command creates a scheduled action with the following parameters:

#

Argument

Description

Example

`[0]`

StartTime

When this command can run from

`"01/11/2024 10:30:00"`

`[1]`

EndTime

When this command will stop running

`"08/11/2024 10:30:00"`

`[2]`

RepeatTime

The time interval between each time this command runs

`"01:00:00"`

`[3]`

RepeatAmount

How many times this command will run

`24`

`[4]`

Command

The command you want to run

`say`

`[5]`

CommandParams

The parameters for your chosen command

`"Join our discord!"`

circle-exclamation

Please note, all times used in The Scheduler commands are in UTC with date format DD/MM/YYYY and time format HH:MM:SS.

circle-info

If you make the command repeat, the end time will automatically adjust to when the command will be done repeating

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/command-scheduling#example)

Example

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/command-scheduling#undefined)
> 
> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/command-scheduling#createaction-convarscheduleraction-01-11-2024-10-30-00-15-06-2025-19-55-00-00-01-00-10-say-welcome)
> 
> CreateAction ConVarSchedulerAction "01/11/2024 10:30:00" "15/06/2025 19:55:00" "00:01:00" 10 say "Welcome"
> 
> This will run the "say" command every minute (which will put the text "Welcome" in the game chat), 10 times, starting at 10:30 UTC on November 1st 2024.

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/command-scheduling#listactions)

listactions

The `listactions`command will return all created Scheduler actions with their IDs

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FnN0SE95lE6zS0rq1ousU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc2837a5f-82bb-4cf8-9680-274d7b6a0ccf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=39b8dca&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/command-scheduling#removeaction)

removeaction

The `removeaction` command will delete the action whose ID you input

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/command-scheduling#example-1)

Example

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/command-scheduling#undefined-1)
> 
> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/command-scheduling#removeaction-3)
> 
> removeaction 3
> 
> This will delete the action with the ID 3

[PreviousModeration Actionschevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions)
[NextCustom Zoneschevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/custom-zones)

Last updated 5 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [listactions](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/command-scheduling#listactions)
    
*   [removeaction](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/command-scheduling#removeaction)
