# Moderation Actions | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

The Player Actions menu is located within the Player List.

When selecting a player, Moderators/Admins/Owners have a suite of options for dealing with players who they feel are breaking rules.

The Player Actions menu does _not_ require a prior reporting action, and can be executed at any time.

These options are:

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions#report-player)

Report Player


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This option will send a report to the Admins/Owners, so that a disciplinary action may be taken and a report can be made for tracking purposes.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions#block-player)

Block Player


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This option will completely block communication between the target player and yourself, so that they are not able to communicate with you in any way.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions#kick-player)

Kick Player


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This option is identical to the option presented to Admins in the \[Inbox\], but does not require a report prior to taking action.

This option temporarily boots the player from the server, usually as a warning to the target player.

The target is able to rejoin the server after being kicked, probably with a more humble attitude.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions#disable-communication)

Disable Communication


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This option is identical to the option presented to Admins in the \[Inbox\], but does not require a report prior to taking action.

This action will disable Voice Chat, Quick Chat (Text), or both.

Admins can undo this by re-selecting this option and selecting \[Enable Communication\].

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions#give-warning)

Give Warning


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This option is identical to the option presented to Admins in the \[Inbox\], but does not require a report prior to taking action.

This option will issue a warning to the target player, which will be applied to them the next time they join the server.

The target will receive a pop-up on join telling them that they have been warned, and informs them that they may be banned if they continue breaking rules.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions#teleport)

Teleport


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This option allows the Admin to immediately teleport to the target players location, so that the Admin can actively monitor the target player. (This is best used in conjunction with GodMode/NoClip/Vanish)

The Admin also has the option to teleport a target to themselves, potentially to put them in “jail” or give them a verbal warning through in-game chat.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions#kick-and-ban)

Kick and Ban


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In addition to kicking a player, this option will also ban the player for a chosen amount of time.

The current options for timescales are:

*   6 Hours
    
*   24 Hours
    
*   1 Week
    
*   Permanent
    

Like standard bans on official servers, the player will be given a popup telling them that they have been banned from that particular server, but they will be free to join other Community Servers if they choose.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions#change-role)

Change role


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here, you have the option to promote/demote players to different levels.

*   Promote to VIP
    
*   Promote to Moderator
    
*   Promote to Admin
    
*   Promote to Owner (Owners only)
    
    *   Practice care with this command, as multiple owners on a server can expose your account to being demoted by someone else. This can be reverted through the G-Portal page if you are the true Owner)
        
    

Players who have been promoted will immediately have access to the features of that level, without having to rejoin.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions#spectate)

Spectate


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This option allows Mods/Admins/Owners to spectate the chosen player.

*   Only Admins/Owners can manipulate targets’ items, like dropping items from their inventory, moving them around, or deleting them completely.
    
*   Moderators have a more basic Spectate mode, and they are not allowed to manipulate items.
    

[PreviousConfiguration Backupschevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup/configuration-backups)
[NextCommand Schedulingchevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/command-scheduling)

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Block Player](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions#block-player)
    
*   [Kick Player](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions#kick-player)
    
*   [Disable Communication](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions#disable-communication)
    
*   [Give Warning](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions#give-warning)
    
*   [Teleport](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/moderation-actions#teleport)

# Logs, Booting & Saving | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/logs-booting-and-saving#logs)

Logs


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In GPORTAL | NITRADO, this page contains the server’s log file, public.log.

This server outputs the following information to the file:

*   Boot Details
    
*   Save Status
    
*   Player Joining and Leaving
    
*   Authority Levels
    
*   Populations
    
*   Event Details
    

Server owners are given the option to download the log files for troubleshooting, monitoring, and posterity purposes. The public.log file can be opened in any text editor, but for large files taken from busy servers, we recommend using something like Notepad++.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.squarespace-cdn.com%2Fcontent%2Fv1%2F602d246245658135031e4b2a%2F93004f55-6e84-4377-81dc-3e8e9a4ee25e%2Flogs-01.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74ab97a5&sv=2)

The GPORTAL Server Log

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FZad4EI3rX4I3fNaIoKwe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D103483bb-1bbf-49a1-908f-9afde910c814&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ea142a07&sv=2)

The NITRADO Server Log

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/logs-booting-and-saving#console)

Console


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The console page displays the public.log file, but allows server owners to enter commands at will.

For example, the owner can check the status of any command they have entered by simply typing the command into the console, and it will provide a response displaying the current status.

You can also check the server’s health during boot and save phases.

circle-exclamation

_**When booting a server, please wait for 10-15 minutes as the server works silently at some points. This may look like the server is frozen, but it’s not!**_

circle-check

_GPORTAL and NITRADO servers both boot identically. In this page, only GPORTAL is shown._

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/logs-booting-and-saving#booting-phase)

Booting phase

During the server boot, the set of messages shown in the below image will be displayed in the console.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.squarespace-cdn.com%2Fcontent%2Fv1%2F602d246245658135031e4b2a%2F3ae33548-4f8e-47a4-b556-77d397a3e027%2Flogs-02.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=110c00dd&sv=2)

This process will seem like it has frozen at points, but do not restart the server or make any changes until the server has fully booted.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.squarespace-cdn.com%2Fcontent%2Fv1%2F602d246245658135031e4b2a%2F3ea6771e-1cd6-4971-9444-12cd3611e2bf%2Flogs-03.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=297fb5d7&sv=2)

After this message has appeared, you are able to join the server, make changes, and tinker with settings.

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/logs-booting-and-saving#saves)

Saves

When the server saves, this following message will be displayed in the console. This stream of messages appears every 5 minutes as the server saves its current state.

This can also be triggered manually by entering “save” into the console.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.squarespace-cdn.com%2Fcontent%2Fv1%2F602d246245658135031e4b2a%2F0afb8e6e-63ff-407c-9c2d-e67bfcd261ee%2Flogs-04.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c2a30bfb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/logs-booting-and-saving#entering-commands)

Entering commands

Users can enter any command at any time into the console, and the console will return the associated information about the command:

Let’s say we would like create a new Starter Kit, using the command shown in the [Kit Management](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management)
section.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.squarespace-cdn.com%2Fcontent%2Fv1%2F602d246245658135031e4b2a%2F02aca0af-43b2-4efa-873c-31ece864a85a%2Flogs-05.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a039406a&sv=2)

The intended action for this command is to add an Assault Rifle to a new starter kit called “TestKit”, in the Hotbar (Belt) section of the players inventory.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.squarespace-cdn.com%2Fcontent%2Fv1%2F602d246245658135031e4b2a%2Fe669005f-1850-470e-966c-8b34ee357fb0%2Flogs-06.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8d0d926c&sv=2)

As you can see, we have been successful in adding the item to the Kit. In order for this kit to spawn in a players inventory, we must enter a few more commands.

First, let’s check the status of the new Kit we just created:

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.squarespace-cdn.com%2Fcontent%2Fv1%2F602d246245658135031e4b2a%2Fcd419867-90f4-4d65-b936-4b3080cf1496%2Flogs-07.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a4f66eec&sv=2)

As shown above, the Assault Rifle has been correctly placed into the new kit, in the Belt area.

For spawning this Kit on a player’s inventory, we have one last command to enter. In this example, let’s say we want all Moderators to spawn with this new Kit.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.squarespace-cdn.com%2Fcontent%2Fv1%2F602d246245658135031e4b2a%2F3e2120d3-c0ae-4c4f-a335-7d72cb5b8170%2Flogs-08.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=606b951d&sv=2)

Success! Now, all Moderators will spawn with an Assault Rifle in their hotbar.

[PreviousGranting User Tierschevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/granting-user-tiers)
[NextRestarts and Backupchevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup)

# Entity Details | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

**Entity details will allow you to access information regarding who built the entity, how long it has been there for and who has access to it. This should help server owners with server moderation.**

To access Entity Details:

1.  Click TRIANGLE+CROSS (or A + Y) to get access to the Control Panel.
    
2.  Scroll down to \[Entity Options\] and set it to \[ON\].
    
3.  Back out of the Control Panel.
    

You should now see the Entity Details UI. This will show information such as entity name, Entity ID, Building ID, Creator ID, Creation Time and when viewing a Tool Cupboard, a list of authorised players will also appear.

By pressing \[LT/L2\] you will enter \[Delete Mode\]. \[RT/R2\] will allow you to completely destroy an entity.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FFgtAuBmhGbXVdyGsEgNd%252FAdminhammer_1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17fc1892-a97f-472b-b410-41e2f9a672e8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c102ce44&sv=2)

[PreviousCustom Zoneschevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/custom-zones)
[Next✨NEW✨ Entity Spawningchevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/new-entity-spawning)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Item Settings | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

This area controls the spawning of items, loot scaling, and blueprint options for all players in the server.

These settings are especially useful for creating 2x/3x loot servers.

triangle-exclamation

_**Keep in mind that spawning excessive amounts of items on the server can lead to server lag, crashes, and client instability due to console hardware limitations.**_

Here, you can customise the following settings to your liking, below are all the options and a summary of each one.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#quick-reference)

Quick reference


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Option

Description

No Starting Items

Toggles the removal of the Rock and Torch when a player spawns.

Builder’s Paradise Items

Toggles the starting kit for a Builder’s Paradise server. (Hammer and Building Plan)

Target Practice Items

Toggles the starting kit for a Target Practice server.

Free Crafting

Toggles the ability to craft without consuming resources.

Instant Crafting

Toggles the ability to instantly craft items.

Unlock All Blueprints

Toggles the unlocking of all blueprints for everyone in the server, meaning that everyone can craft everything.

Workbench Override

Grants all players in the game access to the selected Workbench Aura, allowing them to craft Workbench items anywhere in the map.

Stackable Size Scale

Controls the maximum stack size for all stackable items.

Gather Scale

This controls how much a player will gather from harvestable nodes, trees, and nodettes.

Loot Scale

This controls how much a player will gather from loot boxes, crates, barrels and scientists.

Disable Item Damage

Toggles the "condition" of items (green bar). When enabled, items will last forever and will not need repairs.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#no-starting-items)

No Starting Items


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles the removal of the Rock and Torch when a player spawns.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#input)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#notes)

**Notes**

Activating this is essential if you wish to have \[Builder’s Paradise\] or \[Target Practice\] items activated.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#restart-required)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#builders-paradise-items)

Builder’s Paradise Items


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles the starting kit for a Builder’s Paradise server. (Hammer and Building Plan)

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#input-1)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#notes-1)

**Notes**

It is recommended to only have \[Builder's Paradise Items\] or \[Target Practice Items\] activated at any time, otherwise you will spawn with too many items for the inventory to handle.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#restart-required-1)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#target-practice-items)

Target Practice Items


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles the starting kit for a Target Practice server.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#input-2)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#notes-2)

**Notes**

It is recommended to only have \[Builder's Paradise Items\] or \[Target Practice Items\] activated at any time, otherwise you will spawn with too many items for the inventory to handle.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#restart-required-2)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#free-crafting)

Free Crafting


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles the ability to craft without consuming resources.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#input-3)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#notes-3)

**Notes**

When combined with \[Instant Crafting\], \[Workbench Override 3\], and \[Unlock All Blueprints\], players can instantly craft any item in the game for free, instantly.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#restart-required-3)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#instant-crafting)

Instant Crafting


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles the ability to instantly craft items.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#input-4)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#restart-required-4)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#unlock-all-blueprints)

Unlock All Blueprints


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles the unlocking of all blueprints for everyone in the server, meaning that everyone can craft everything.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#input-5)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#notes-4)

**Notes**

Keep in mind that you will still need the appropriate \[Workbench Override\] to craft Workbench items.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#restart-required-5)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#workbench-override)

Workbench Override


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Grants all players in the game access to the selected Workbench Aura, allowing them to craft Workbench items anywhere in the map.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#input-6)

**Input**

Any number from 0 → 3.

Default is 0.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#restart-required-6)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#stackable-size-scale)

Stackable Size Scale


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the maximum stack size for all stackable items.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#input-7)

**Input**

Any number from 1 → 3.

Default is 1.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#notes-5)

**Notes**

This options are especially effective when combined with \[Gather Scale\].

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#restart-required-7)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#gather-scale)

Gather Scale


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This controls how much a player will gather from harvestable nodes, trees, and nodettes.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#input-8)

**Input**

Any number from 1 → 3.

Default is 1.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#notes-6)

**Notes**

These options are especially effective when combined with \[Stackable Size Scale\]

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#restart-required-8)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#loot-scale)

Loot Scale


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This controls how much a player will gather from loot boxes, crates, barrels and scientists.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#input-9)

####

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#restart-required-9)

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#disable-item-damage)

Disable Item Damage


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles the “condition” of items (green bar). When enabled, items will last forever and will not need repairs.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings#input-10)

# Whitelist Management | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

When enabled, the whitelist is a list of players who can access the server. All other players will be blocked.

The player ID is the gamertag/username of the player on XBOX or PlayStation. You do not need to specify the platform when adding a user to the whitelist.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/whitelist-management#whitelist-activation)

Whitelist Activation


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/whitelist-management#undefined)
> 
> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/whitelist-management#server.enablewhitelist-0-1)
> 
> _server.enablewhitelist "0/1"_
> 
> _Toggles the server's whitelist._

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/whitelist-management#whitelist-viewing)

Whitelist Viewing


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/whitelist-management#undefined-1)
> 
> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/whitelist-management#global.whitelist)
> 
> _global.whitelist_
> 
> This command prints the current whitelist to the console log, if it has been enabled.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/whitelist-management#whitelist-management)

Whitelist Management


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/whitelist-management#undefined-2)
> 
> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/whitelist-management#server.whitelistid-id)
> 
> _server.whitelistID "ID"_
> 
> This command adds the target player to the Whitelist, where "ID" is the in-game name of the chosen player.

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/whitelist-management#undefined-3)
> 
> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/whitelist-management#server.removewhitelist-id)
> 
> _server.removewhitelist "ID"_
> 
> This command aremoves the target player from the Whitelist, where "ID" is the in-game name of the chosen player.

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/whitelist-management#undefined-4)
> 
> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/whitelist-management#global.clearwhitelist)
> 
> _global.clearwhitelist_
> 
> This command clears all players from the whitelist.
> 
> **NOTE**: This will not change whether the whitelist remains active, so make sure to set `server.enablewhitelist "0"` to go back to an open server.

[PreviousServer Tagschevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/server-tags)
[NextGameplaychevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/gameplay)

# Authority Levels & Privileges | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

In order to have control of your server in-game, you must first assign your GamerTag \[XBOX\] or PSN ID \[PlayStation\] to be an Owner in the Boot Commands. Go to the custom boot commands section, or the Console and enter:

Copy

    OwnerID "Gamertag/PSNID" 

circle-check

If your Gamertag or PSN ID has a space in the name, you need to put your name between "quotation marks".

circle-info

If you set yourself as owner, you can't give any other role to yourself.

_**Keep in mind, Owners have all the permissions from Admins and Moderators.**_

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges#user-tiers-explained)

User Tiers Explained


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Our game server offers a tiered user system to provide a structured and customisable experience for different types of players and administrators.

Understanding these tiers will help you manage your server more effectively.

chevron-rightTier 0 - User[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges#tier-0-user)

**Description**

*   The User tier represents the standard player base.
    
*   These are members of the general public who play Rust.
    
*   Any player can become a User on your server, subject to the privacy settings you have configured.
    

**Capabilities**

*   Users can access and play on the server under the rules and conditions set by higher-tiered members.
    
*   They do not possess any special privileges or access rights.
    

**Typical Use**

*   Ideal for the vast majority of players who will interact with your server in a typical gameplay setting.
    

* * *

chevron-rightTier 1 - VIP[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges#tier-1-vip)

**Description**

*   VIPs are a step above regular users.
    
*   This tier is ideal for players whom you wish to recognise or provide with a slightly enhanced experience.
    

**Capabilities**

*   VIPs do not have special in-game rights or permissions.
    
*   They have the ability to skip server queues, ensuring faster access even during peak times.
    

**Typical Use**

*   Suitable for friends, loyal players, or groups you want to encourage to frequently return to the server.
    
*   This tier helps build a dedicated community.
    

* * *

chevron-rightTier 2 - Moderator[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges#tier-2-moderator)

**Description**

*   Moderators are entrusted with maintaining a positive and fair gaming environment on the server.
    

**Capabilities**

*   They can enforce server rules, moderate communications, and have the authority to kick or temporarily ban disruptive players.
    
*   They cannot alter server settings or configurations.
    

**Typical Use**

*   Assign this role to trusted players or community members who can help manage day-to-day interactions and ensure a smooth gaming experience for all.
    

* * *

chevron-rightTier 3 - Admin[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges#tier-3-admin)

**Description**

*   Admins have substantial control over the server and its settings.
    
*   They play a crucial role in managing the technical and gameplay aspects of the server.
    

**Capabilities**

*   Admins can modify server settings, manage user permissions, initiate server-wide events, and handle critical issues like cheating or bugs.
    
*   They also have the power to permanently ban players if necessary.
    

**Typical Use**

*   This role is typically reserved for those who are deeply involved in the server's operation, such as trusted community leaders or team members responsible for server management.
    

* * *

chevron-rightTier 4 - Owner[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges#tier-4-owner)

**Description**

*   The Owner tier represents the highest level of control and access on the server.
    

**Capabilities**

*   Owners have full administrative rights, including server configuration, user management, and the ability to assign or revoke any roles.
    
*   They have the ultimate say in all decisions regarding the server.
    

**Typical Use**

*   This role is exclusively for the individual or group who owns and is responsible for the overall maintenance and direction of the server. Exercise caution when adding players (other than yourself) to this role.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges#privileges)

Privileges


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

User

VIP

Moderator

Administrator

Owner

*   **Skip queue:** No
    
*   **Control panel access:** No
    
*   **Grant Level:** This is the default, no command is needed
    
*   **Revoke level:** N/A
    
*   **Access:** No special privileges. A standard player.
    

*   **Skip queue:** Yes
    
*   **Control panel access:** No
    
*   **Grant Level:** VIPID "GamerTag/PSNID"
    
*   **Revoke level:** RemoveVIP "GamerTag/PSNID"
    
*   **Access:** A standard player, but VIPs can skip to the front of server queues.
    

*   **Skip queue:** Yes
    
*   **Control panel access:** Limited
    
*   **Grant Level:** ModeratorID "GamerTag/PSNID"
    
*   **Revoke level:** RemoveModerator "GamerTag/PSNID"
    
*   **Access:** All VIP privileges, plus:
    
    *   User Moderation Functions: Kicking, Banning, Muting
        
    *   Teleporting to players/locations
        
    *   Control Panel Options
        
    *   GodMode
        
    *   Vanish Mode
        
    *   NoClip Mode
        
    *   Player Spectating
        
    *   Item Spawning List
        
    *   Console Log (public.log) access
        
    

*   **Skip queue:** Yes
    
*   **Control panel access:** Yes
    
*   **Grant Level:** AdminID "GamerTag/PSNID"
    
*   **Revoke level:** RemoveAdmin "GamerTag/PSNID"
    
*   **Access:** All Moderator privileges, plus:
    
    *   In-Game Commands List
        
    *   Time Control
        
    *   Debug Camera
        
    *   Attack Heli on-demand
        
    *   Advanced Destruction Commands
        
    *   Admin Report System
        
    *   Promotion/Demotion Rights
        
    *   Advanced Spectate
        
    *   Custom Commands Input
        
    

*   **Skip queue:** Yes
    
*   **Control panel access:** Yes
    
*   **Grant Level:** OwnerID "GamerTag/PSNID"
    
*   **Revoke level:** RemoveOwner "GamerTag/PSNID"
    
*   **Access:** All Admin Privileges, plus:
    
    *   Full Server-side control
        
    *   Full GPORTAL | NITRADO control
        
    

[PreviousGameplay Settingschevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings)
[NextCustom Auth Levelschevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges/custom-auth-levels)

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [User Tiers Explained](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges#user-tiers-explained)
    
*   [Privileges](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/authority-levels-and-privileges#privileges)

# Gameplay Settings | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

This section controls various aspects of gameplay relating to base construction, upkeep, and decay, as well as damage from different types of weapons.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#quick-reference)

Quick reference


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Option

Description

Demolish Time

Controls the amount of time after a building block is built that it can be demolished for free.

Demolish Hammer

Toggles the Demolish ability for the Hammer, allowing it to immediately destroy any building block you own.

Free Upgrading

Toggles the ability to upgrade building blocks without consuming resources.

Free Construction

Toggles the ability to build structures without consuming resources. A Building Plan is still required by the player.

Bullet Damage

Controls the amount of damage done by bullets.

Bleeding Damage

Controls the amount of damage done by bleeding.

Arrow Damage

Controls the amount of damage done by arrows.

Melee Damage

Controls the amount of damage done by melee attacks.

Decay Scale

Controls the amount of decay for player structures that occurs over time.

Upkeep

Toggles the requirement to keep resources in your Tool Cupboard to stop it from decaying.

Grief Protection

Controls the time that a structure is protected by a Tool Cupboard after the TC is destroyed.

Decay Tick

Controls how often decay damage is calculated and dealt to player-made structures.

Code Lock Maximum Failed Attempts

Controls the maximum amount of incorrect attempts on a Code Lock before it rejects further attempts.

Code Lock Lockout Cooldown

When the Failed Attempts value has been reached, this controls how long the player is locked out for before being able to re-attempt a Code Lock.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#demolish-time)

Demolish Time


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the amount of time after a building block is built that it can be demolished for free.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#input)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² (essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#notes)

**Notes**

Time is measured in real-world seconds.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#restart-required)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#demolish-hammer)

Demolish Hammer


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles the Demolish ability for the Hammer, allowing it to immediately destroy any building block you own with the \[Right Trigger / R2\]

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#input-1)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#restart-required-1)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#free-upgrading)

Free Upgrading


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles the ability to upgrade building blocks without consuming resources.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#input-2)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#restart-required-2)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#free-construction)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles the ability to build structures without consuming resources.

A Building Plan is still required by the player.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#input-3)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#restart-required-3)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#bullet-damage)

Bullet Damage


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the amount of damage done by bullets.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#input-4)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² (essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#notes-1)

**Notes**

Useful for Target Practice servers, or creation of insta-gib servers.

2 = double bullet damage (includes NPCs, Attack Heli, and Bradley APC)

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#restart-required-4)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#bleeding-damage)

Melee Damage


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the amount of damage done by melee attacks.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#input-7)

Decay Scale


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the amount of decay for player structures that occurs over time.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#input-8)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² (essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#notes-5)

**Notes**

Set this to 0 if you would like buildings to never decay under any circumstances.

triangle-exclamation

_Beware of potential instability if there are too many buildings on your server that aren’t decaying._

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#restart-required-8)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#upkeep)

Upkeep


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles the requirement to keep resources in your Tool Cupboard to stop it from decaying.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#input-9)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default ON.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#notes-6)

**Notes**

Disable this if you like building to stand forever without anything in your Tool Cupboard.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#restart-required-9)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#grief-protection)

Grief Protection


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the time that a structure is protected by a Tool Cupboard after the TC is destroyed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#input-10)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² (essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#notes-7)

**Notes**

Time is measured in real-world seconds.

Set this to 0 if you would like bases to start decaying immediately after the Tool Cupboard is destroyed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#restart-required-10)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#decay-tick)

Decay Tick


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls how often decay damage is calculated and dealt to player-made structures.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#input-11)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² (essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#notes-8)

**Notes**

Setting this extremely high will cause buildings to decay almost instantly, especially if Decay Scale is also set to a high value.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#restart-required-11)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#code-lock-maximum-failed-attempts)

Code Lock Maximum Failed Attempts


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the maximum amount of incorrect attempts on a Code Lock before it rejects further attempts.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#input-12)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² (essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#notes-9)

**Notes**

Set this extremely high if you would don’t want to be locked of out of Code Locks at all.

Useful if you would like to allow for Code Raiding on your server.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#restart-required-12)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#code-lock-lockout-cooldown)

Code Lock Lockout Cooldown


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When the \[Failed Attempts\] value has been reached, this controls how long the player is locked out for before being able to re-attempt a Code Lock.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#input-13)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² (essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#notes-10)

**Notes**

Set this to 0 for no cooldown, meaning that players can attempt without penalty.

Time is measured in real-world seconds.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings#restart-required-13)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

# Granting User Tiers | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/granting-user-tiers#viewing-and-managing-user-tiers)

Viewing and managing user tiers


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/granting-user-tiers#id-1.-log-in-to-your-gportal-or-nitrado-account)

**1\. Log in to Your GPORTAL | NITRADO Account**

**Action**

*   Open your web browser and navigate to the GPORTAL | NITRADO website.
    

**Details**

*   Log in using your GPORTAL | NITRADO account credentials.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/granting-user-tiers#id-2.-access-your-server-dashboard)

**2\. Access Your Server Dashboard**

**Action**

*   Once logged in, go to the 'My Servers' section.
    

**Details**

*   Here, you'll see a list of all the servers you have rented. Select the server you wish to manage.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/granting-user-tiers#id-3.-select-a-server-and-navigate-to-user-management)

**3\. Select a Server and Navigate to User Management**

**Action**

*   After selecting a server, select either basic settings or console from the menu on the left hand side.
    

**Details**

*   From either of these sections of the server management page you can enter commands to grant permissions. The exact commands to Grant and Revoke Levels are listed below for each tier of player
    

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/granting-user-tiers#id-4.-set-permission-via-console-page)

**4\. Set permission via console page**

**Action**

*   From the tab menu at the top of the server page, select _**Console.**_ Here you can enter either the grant or revoke commands, one at a time.
    

**Details**

*   These permissions will be granted or revoked without a server restart. Make sure to clear any unused authorisations from the Boot Commands section if you have any.
    

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/granting-user-tiers#grant-commands)

Grant commands


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

VIP

Moderator

Administrator

Owner

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/granting-user-tiers#revoke-commands)

Revoke commands


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

VIP

Moderator

Administrator

Owner

# Restarts and Backup | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#restarts)

Restarts


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

triangle-exclamation

_**It is strongly recommended to set a regular wipe schedule! Servers without a scheduled wipe every month (at least) will be prone to instability, client crashes and server crashes.**_

This page provides multiple options for scheduled wipe times, daily restarts, etc.

You will be presented with the following options:

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.squarespace-cdn.com%2Fcontent%2Fv1%2F602d246245658135031e4b2a%2Fc3ac37e4-fc81-4459-b509-cfb4e110dcd6%2Frestarts-01.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d2ce3987&sv=2)

The GPORTAL Scheduling Page

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252F1ZRlj397EmxIWuXFJAX9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90a84989-2db8-4ed6-8658-3fad045ecc7c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5cc3231d&sv=2)

The NITRADO Scheduling Page

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#schedule)

Schedule

This controls how often the server will restart automatically.

*   Daily (essential for creating backups)
    
*   Weekly
    
*   Bi-Monthly (every 2 weeks) (GPORTAL only)
    
*   Monthly
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#day-of-month)

Day of month

This determines which day the server will restart.

*   First Day of the Month
    
*   Middle of the Month
    
*   Last Day of the Month
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#time-of-day)

Time of day

This controls what time the server will restart

*   This is in GMT, so make sure to adjust for your time-zone accordingly!
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#description)

Description

This is a reference for the Owner.

*   Appears on GPORTAL only
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#wipe-type)

Wipe type

This controls what happens when the server restarts.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#save-wipe)

Save Wipe

*   Only erases player buildings/inventories.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#blueprint-wipe)

Blueprint Wipe

*   Erases Blueprint/Tech Tree progress.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#full-wipe)

Full Wipe

*   Combines both of the above options for a complete reset of all progress.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#creating-a-daily-restart)

Creating a daily restart

To create a daily restart, simply enter the following into the input boxes:

**Schedule**

*   Daily
    

**Time of Day**

*   Your preferred time (GMT)
    

**Description**

*   Daily Restart
    

**Wipe Type**

*   No Wipe
    

After this has been created, the Backups option will become available to you.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#backups)

Backups


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

triangle-exclamation

_**It is strongly recommended to create regular backups of your server! Servers without automatic backups can lead to loss of progress and client instability.**_

The Backups page is a very useful tool, especially for busy servers.

Here, you can enable Automatic Backups, which will save your server’s current form every time the server is restarted through the _**Restarts**_ system.

You can have up to 3 daily restarts active at once, or you can create any amount of manual backup, provided you have the storage space available.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#creating-an-automatic-server-backup)

Creating an automatic server backup

1.  Set up an **automatic daily restart** on your server
    
2.  Enable the toggle at the top of the _**Backups**_ page
    
3.  You’re done! The server will now save a backup every time the server restarts (daily)
    

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.squarespace-cdn.com%2Fcontent%2Fv1%2F602d246245658135031e4b2a%2F0a45fc5b-1e94-453a-8218-b9ca951cc084%2Fbackups-01.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9cca35c9&sv=2)

GPORTAL Automatic Backups

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FHSN3mGbQZL1TXFbrsp7S%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D48e7bb43-9846-47f1-a725-3a67cb275a5b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5a6626d6&sv=2)

NITRADO Automatic Backups

* * *

circle-exclamation

_NITRADO currently does not provide the option to back up your server manually._

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#creating-a-manual-server-backup-gportal-only)

Creating a manual server backup (GPORTAL Only)

1.  Set up an **automatic daily restart** on your server
    
2.  Press the \[Create a Backup\] button
    
3.  Follow the prompt, and continue
    
4.  Wait for the server backup to be created
    
5.  You’re done! The server now has a backup that you can restore any time
    

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.squarespace-cdn.com%2Fcontent%2Fv1%2F602d246245658135031e4b2a%2Fc85a0f2b-3fb8-439a-b312-dcd6c63a2b86%2Fbackups-02.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=93b2a9d0&sv=2)

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.squarespace-cdn.com%2Fcontent%2Fv1%2F602d246245658135031e4b2a%2F690c7080-c05e-45ef-83b7-dd2d800e0271%2Fbackups-03.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e7fa9ead&sv=2)

[PreviousLogs, Booting & Savingchevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/logs-booting-and-saving)
[NextConfiguration Backupschevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup/configuration-backups)

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Restarts](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#restarts)
    
*   [Schedule](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#schedule)
    
*   [Day of month](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/management-settings/restarts-and-backup#day-of-month)

# Seasonal Events | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#seasonal-events-can-now-be-controlled-by-server-owners)

**Seasonal Events can now be controlled by server owners!**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

Please note, activating an event will cause all players in a server to be kicked, while the server sets up the event. You do not need to restart your server to activate custom events.

circle-exclamation

These values are case sensitive.

circle-exclamation

Changing between event types (Xmas -> Halloween, etc.) will destroy all items (including deployables) from the previous event, but activating multiple events of the same type (Xmas + Xmas Portals) will not.

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#using-the-gportal-options-page)

Using the GPORTAL Options page

When initially setting up your seasonal events, you must use the GPORTAL Options dropdown, located in the "Events" section.

This will ensure that your chosen event(s) will always be running on your server, regardless of wipes and restarts.

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#using-seasonal-events-commands)

Using Seasonal Events commands

After you have set up the seasonal events on your server through the GPORTAL page, you are now free to manipulate the events through the GPORTAL console, using the commands listed on this page.

These commands will not affect the server if it wipes or restarts, and will only persist while the server is still running. If the events are not specified by using the dropdown, they will be removed on restart.

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#example-combining-options-and-commands)

Example: Combining Options and Commands

Let's say you want to create a permanent Halloween server. You would use the option in the GPORTAL page, restart the server, and the event will then be "baked in" to the server's configuration so that it persists across restarts.

Midwipe, you want to change the event to Xmas. You can do this without restarting by entering the following command into the GPORTAL console: `events.start_special Xmas`.

circle-exclamation

_**NOTE:**_

_**This action will kick all players currently in the server while it prepares the event, but will not restart the server. The specified event will not persist through restarts or wipes unless added to the GPORTAL page dropdown.**_

You can also pause and unpause the seasonal events without restarting by using the commands listed below in the GPORTAL Console.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#list-of-events)

List of Events


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#undefined)
> 
> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#events.list_special)
> 
> _events.list\_special_
> 
> Lists all available events.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#event-check)

Event Check


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#undefined-1)
> 
> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#events.current_special)
> 
> _events.current\_special_
> 
> Prints the current Seasonal Event to the console log.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#event-pause)

Event Pause


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#undefined-2)
> 
> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#events.pause_special-1)
> 
> _events.pause\_special_ `1`
> 
> Stops the event from occurring, but preserves deployables.
> 
> Does not kick players, just stops the events from occurring.
> 
> Pausing during an active event will immediately stop that event from occurring.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#event-unpause)

Event Unpause


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#undefined-3)
> 
> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#events.pause_special-0)
> 
> _events.pause\_special_ `0`
> 
> Restarts the event that you just paused.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#event-types)

Event Types


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#easter)

Easter

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#undefined-4)
> 
> **📟🌌**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#events.start_special-easter)
> 
> _events.start\_special_ `Easter`
> 
> Activates the Easter Collection Event.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#halloween)

Halloween

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#undefined-5)
> 
> **📟🌌**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#events.start_special-halloween)
> 
> _events.start\_special_ `Halloween`
> 
> Activates the Halloween Collection Event.

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#undefined-6)
> 
> **📟🌌**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#events.start_special-halloweenportal)
> 
> _events.start\_special_ `HalloweenPortal`
> 
> Activates the Halloween Portals.

circle-exclamation

Executing `pause_special 1` then `pause_special 0` while Portals are active will destroy them immediately and change their position.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#xmas)

Xmas

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#undefined-7)
> 
> **📟🌌**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#events.start_special-xmas)
> 
> _events.start\_special_ `Xmas`
> 
> Activates the Christmas Collection Event.

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#undefined-8)
> 
> **📟🌌**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#events.start_special-xmasportal)
> 
> _events.start\_special_ `XmasPortal`
> 
> Activates the Christmas Portals.

circle-exclamation

Executing `pause_special 1` then `pause_special 0` while Portals are active will destroy them immediately and change their position.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#example)

Example

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#undefined-9)
> 
> **📟🌌**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#events.start_special-xmas-1)
> 
> _events.start\_special_ `Xmas`
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#events.start_special-xmasportal-1)
> 
> _events.start\_special_ `XmasPortal`
> 
> When entered separately into the GPORTAL console, these commands will activate both types of Xmas Event (Collection and Portals).

triangle-exclamation

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events#xmas-type-events-and-halloween-type-events-cannot-be-simultaneously-active-on-a-server)

_**Xmas-type events and Halloween-type events cannot be simultaneously active on a server!**_
