# Player Settings | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

This section controls the behaviours of the players, their health, and their interactions with other players.

Here, you can customise the following settings to your liking, below are all the options and a summary each one.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#quick-reference)

Quick reference


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-check

For True PvE Mode, change the following settings: **\- PvP Mode:** `**OFF**` **- PvB Mode:** `**OFF**`

Option

Description

Immortal Server

Toggles damage on the server.

Game Mode

Selects a game mode for the server to run. **NOTE:** changing this option will cause a full map/BP wipe!

PvP Mode

Toggles PvP mode, meaning players can deal damage to each other.

PvB Mode

Toggles PvB mode, meaning players can deal damage to other players' buildings.

Infinite Ammo

Toggles infinite ammunition for weapons.

Full Starting Magazine

Toggles a full magazine when you start with a weapon.

Max Health

Controls the maximum health of a player.

Starting Health (Max)

Controls the maximum starting health for a player when they wake up.

Starting Health (Min)

Controls the minimum starting health for a player when they wake up.

Max Team Size

Controls the maximum number of players that can be part of a single team.

Limit Building Authorisations

Toggle to limit the amount of authorisations on a Tool Cupboard to the current Team Size.

Limit Turret Authorisations

Toggle to limit the amount of authorisations on Auto Turrets to the current Team Size.

Limit Team Locks

Toggle to limit the amount of authorisations on a Code/Key Locks to the current Team Size.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#immortal-server)

Immortal Server


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles damage on the server.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#input)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#notes)

**Notes**

If disabled, players cannot die under any circumstances.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#restart-required)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#game-mode)

Game Mode


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Selects a game mode for the server.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#input-1)

Input

Drop-down, options are:

*   Vanilla
    
*   Easy Mode
    
*   Hard Mode
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#notes-1)

Notes

**Vanilla**

*   This game mode is the default. All settings remain unchanged.
    

**Easy Mode**

*   This gamemode includes the following features:
    
    *   Loot Saving
        
        *   Half of your items will remain on your corpse until you retrieve them
            
        *   These items cannot be looted by other players
            
        
    *   Reclaim Station
        
        *   Located at the Outpost and Bandit Camp
            
        *   You can reclaim half of your lost items from here when you respawn
            
        *   Items will despawn after 2 hours
            
        
    *   Safe Zone Respawning
        
        *   You can respawn at the Outpost of Bandit Camp
            
        *   (NOTE: This only works if you are not marked as hostile)
            
        
    

**Hard Mode**

*   This gamemode includes the following features:
    
    *   Added:
        
        *   Limit of 5 sleeping bags and beds
            
        *   Local chat only for messages and gestures (100m range)
            
        
    *   Removed:
        
        *   Compass
            
        *   Crawling when wounded
            
        *   Global Message
            
        *   Team System
            
        *   Map
            
        *   Safe Zones
            
        *   Scientists and Turrets at the Outpost & Bandit Camp
            
        *   Mission NPCs
            
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#restart-required-1)

Restart Required?

Yes

triangle-exclamation

_**A full wipe (including map, save, and blueprints) is required to activate or deactivate a server gamemode.**_

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#pvp-mode)

PvP Mode


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles PvP (Player vs Player) mode, meaning players can deal damage to each other.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#input-2)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default ON.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#notes-2)

**Notes**

When deactivated, players can still take damage from NPCs and animals, as well as environmental damage.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#restart-required-2)

**Restart Required?**

No

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#pvb-mode)

PvB Mode


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles PvB (Player vs Building) mode, meaning players can deal damage to other players' buildings.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#input-3)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default ON.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#notes-3)

**Notes**

When activated, players can still deal damage to building blocks that they have created, regardless of TC authorisation.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#restart-required-3)

**Restart Required?**

No

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#infinite-ammo)

Infinite Ammo


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles infinite ammunition for weapons.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#input-4)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#notes-4)

**Notes**

The ammo count in your magazine will not go down.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#restart-required-4)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#full-starting-magazine)

Full Starting Magazine


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles a full magazine when you start with a weapon.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#input-5)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#notes-5)

**Notes**

The default starting ammunition is less than half of a full mag.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#restart-required-5)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#max-health)

Max Health


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the maximum health of a player.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#input-6)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² (essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#notes-6)

**Notes**

This can be useful for testing, as well as “Juggernaut” gamemodes.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#restart-required-6)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#starting-health-max)

Starting Health (Max)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the maximum starting health for a player when they wake up.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#input-7)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² (essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#notes-7)

**Notes**

The default is 60HP.

Set both (min) and (max) to the same number to guarantee that health upon wake-up.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#restart-required-7)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#starting-health-min)

Starting Health (Min)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the minimum starting health for a player when they wake up.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#input-8)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² (essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#notes-8)

**Notes**

The default is 50HP.

Set both (min) and (max) to the same number to guarantee that health upon wake-up.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#restart-required-8)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#max-team-size)

Max Team Size


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the maximum amount of players that can be part of a single team.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#input-9)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 10

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#notes-9)

**Notes**

The default is 8.

This can be useful for solo/duo/trio servers.

Set to 1 to disable teams entirely.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#restart-required-9)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#limit-building-authorisations)

Limit Building Authorisations


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggle to limit the amount of authorisations on a Tool Cupboard to the current Team Size.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#input-10)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#notes-10)

**Notes**

This can be useful for solo/duo/trio servers.

Setting Team Size to 2, and toggling this ON means only 2 people can be authorised on a Tool Cupboard at one time.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#restart-required-10)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#limit-turret-authorisations)

Limit Turret Authorisations


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggle to limit the amount of authorisations on Auto Turrets to the current Team Size.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#input-11)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#notes-11)

**Notes**

This can be useful for solo/duo/trio servers.

Setting Team Size to 2, and toggling this ON means only 2 people can be authorised on an Auto Turret at one time.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#restart-required-11)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#limit-team-locks)

Limit Team Locks


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggle to limit the amount of authorisations on a Code/Key Locks to the current Team Size.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#input-12)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default OFF.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#notes-12)

**Notes**

This can be useful for solo/duo/trio servers.

Setting Team Size to 2, and toggling this ON means only 2 people can be authorised on a Lock at one time.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/player-settings#restart-required-12)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

# ✨NEW✨ Entity Spawning | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

You can spawn the following items with the use of the following command:

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/new-entity-spawning#undefined)
> 
> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/new-entity-spawning#entity.spawn-shortname-position)
> 
> _entity.spawn_ `_shortname_` `_position_`
> 
> Where "entity" is any item on the right of the following list,
> 
> "position" is the `x,y,z` co-ordinates of where you want to place it.
> 
> Leaving the "position" blank will spawn the entity at `0,0,0`.
> 
> Quotation marks are not required for this command.

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/new-entity-spawning#example)

_Example_

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/new-entity-spawning#undefined-1)
> 
> **📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/new-entity-spawning#entity.spawn-2module_car_spawned-100-50-200)
> 
> _entity.spawn_ `_2module_car_spawned_` `_100,50,200_`
> 
> This command will spawn a 2 Module Car (Premade) at the position (100, 50, 200)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/new-entity-spawning#crates)

*   [World Objects](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/new-entity-spawning#world-objects)

# Server Tags | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

circle-info

Please note that Server Tags are applied to your server & official servers automatically, and cannot be turned off

Server Tags appear in the server list, loading screens, and welcome screen. They're linked to the monuments on your server, and certain gameplay settings.

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/server-tags#server-list)

Server List

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FbMSOUU25zBgmWLDAVZMg%252F172.16.4.140_Image_163.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5be1a0d-51d4-408e-b51d-149d87c497b2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f7d8539&sv=2)

You can view all of a server's tags by pressing L1/LB (Show Info).

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252F6NkM6pDjQaE37dFb2xQW%252F172.16.4.140_Image_162.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D65c112fa-8961-490f-9d4e-a4cee84e040e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2fc4214a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/server-tags#tag-filtering)

Tag Filtering

You can now filter servers by their tags. This can be accessed by opening the existing Filter Menu and pressing SQUARE/X to switch to the Tag Filters.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FMvEzQUnTE0XywI6rLRwa%252F172.16.4.140_Image_166.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8068f1c1-d261-4c2a-b0fd-9272e0b92168&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d41eb590&sv=2)

Tags are categorized into Gameplay, Land Monuments, and Offshore Monuments sections for ease of navigation. Currently selected tags appear in the Active section, and you can search for tags to select by pressing TRIANGLE/Y.

circle-info

Please note that searching for the Gather/Loot/Stack Size Scale tags will show all servers where the value is greater than 1

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/server-tags#loading-screen)

Loading Screen

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FCUWwbUxIIkRlaGWq4qgI%252F172.16.4.140_Image_164.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34a19e8a-e76a-42e4-ba1f-bff1511ba649&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=be64252a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/server-tags#welcome-screen)

Welcome Screen

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FP0db6OYtvWwg3cXSHUMa%252F172.16.4.140_Image_165.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5bff991-23b6-466b-8a05-e9d54998bab3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d1c14d9b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/server-tags#gameplay-tags)

Gameplay Tags

Gameplay Tags are blue, appear first in the list of tags, and are the only tags that appear in loading screens.

The following is a list of every Gameplay Tag and the setting that causes it to be applied to your server, in the same order they appear in game:

circle-info

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/server-tags#monument-tags)

Monument Tags

Monument Tags are green, appear after Gameplay Tags in the list of tags, and do not appear in loading screens. They are linked to the monuments that are on your map currently.

circle-info

Remember that even if you select a monument to spawn, it might not spawn on your map, as maps are procedurally generated and random.

# Event Settings | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

Some owners won’t want the Attack Heli or Chinook bothering them if they are trying to run a Building server, so we have provided options for controlling many of the events in the game.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#quick-reference)

Quick reference


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Option

Description

Enable Helicopter to Target Players

Toggles whether the Attack Heli can attack players.

Attack Heli Bullet Accuracy

Controls the aim-cone of the Attack Helicopter.

Attack Heli Damage Scale

Controls the scale of the damage done by the Attack Heli’s main guns.

Enable Bradley

Toggles the Bradley APC spawning function at the Launch Site.

Bradley APC Respawn Delay

Controls the amount of time taken for the Bradley APC to respawn after it has been destroyed.

Locked Crate Decay Time

Controls the amount of time taken for a Locked Crate to disappear if not interacted with. Time is measured in real-world seconds.

Locked Crate Time to Unlock

Controls the amount of time needed to hack a Locked Crate. Time is measured in real-world seconds.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#enable-helicopter-to-target-players)

Enable Helicopter to Target Players


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles whether the Attack Helicopter can attack players.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#input)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default ON.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#restart-required)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#attack-heli-bullet-accuracy)

Attack Heli Bullet Accuracy


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the aim-cone of the Attack Helicopter.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#input-1)

**Input**

Any value from 1 → 360.

360 will enable omni-directional targetting of players by the Attack Helicopter.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#notes)

**Notes**

The value you input into this field controls the “aim-cone” of the Attack Helicopter.

If this is set to 180, the Attack Helicopter will only target players in the front half of its perspective. See the below diagram for a representation of how this works.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FIR33POjqVPD23O9Um8UT%252FheliBullet.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee2232c5-64c7-460a-a699-bad926262553&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7e2457d2&sv=2)

Helicopter aim cone

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#restart-required-1)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#attack-heli-damage-scale)

Attack Heli Damage Scale


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the scale of the damage done by the Attack Heli’s main guns.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#input-2)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² (essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#notes-1)

**Notes**

Can theoretically deal 0 damage, or crank it up to insta-kill.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#restart-required-2)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#enable-bradley)

Enable Bradley


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Toggles the Bradley APC spawning function at the Launch Site.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#input-3)

**Input**

Toggle-able, default ON.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#restart-required-3)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#bradley-apc-respawn-delay)

Bradley APC Respawn Delay


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the amount of time taken for the Bradley APC to respawn after it has been destroyed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#input-4)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² (essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#notes-2)

**Notes**

This is measured in real-world minutes.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#restart-required-4)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#locked-crate-decay-time-to-unlock)

Locked Crate Decay Time to Unlock


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the amount of time taken for a Locked Crate to disappear if not interacted with.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#input-5)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² (essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#notes-3)

**Notes**

Set this very high if you don’t want Locked Crates to decay if they aren’t being interacted with.

Time is measured in real-world seconds.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#restart-required-5)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#locked-crate-hack-time)

Locked Crate Hack Time


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Controls the amount of time needed to hack a Locked Crate.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#input-6)

**Input**

Any number, but this value is clamped to a maximum of 3.4×10³² (essentially infinite).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#notes-4)

**Notes**

Set this to 0 for instant hacking of Locked Crates.

Time is measured in real-world seconds.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#restart-required-6)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#event-settings)

Event Settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following commands are used to control server events.

Available events are:

Event

Event Code

Description

Airdrop

`event_airdrop`

A plane flies over the map and drops a crate of supplies that players can loot. Players can see the crate on the map.

Chinook

`event_cargoheli`

A helicopter manned by scientists will patrol a monument and drop a Locked Crate there. Players can loot the crate, but it will take some time to unlock.

Cargo Ship

`event_cargoship`

A cargo ship passes by the island. If players can make their way to it (using boats or by swimming), they can find loot, but it is protected by hostile scientists.

Attack Helicopter

`event_helicopter`

A helicopter patrols a section of the map. It is hostile to players and will attack on sight. Well-equipped players can destroy it to find loot.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#special-events)

Special Events


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#input-7)

**Input**

Dropdown, with the following options:

*   Easter
    
*   Halloween
    
*   HalloweenPortal
    
*   Xmas
    
*   XmasPortal
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#notes-5)

**Notes**

For more information, please see the [Seasonal Eventsarrow-up-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/rust-console-edition-community-servers/feature-guides/seasonal-events)
 page.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/event-settings#restart-required-7)

**Restart Required?**

Yes

[PreviousItem Settingschevron-left](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/item-settings)
[NextGameplay Settingschevron-right](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/server-configuration/gameplay-settings)

# Modifiers | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

Modifiers allow you to manually edit the gather rates, cook speeds, loot scaling for individual items, and other things.

You can add multiple modifiers for the same item, or of the same type, but each new command will require a new line.

circle-info

_A good resource for “_`_itemname_`_” is_ [_Corrosion hour's guide to Rust_arrow-up-right](https://www.corrosionhour.com/rust-item-list/)
 _Please keep in mind that some items listed on this site may not be implemented in Rust: Console Edition at the time of writing._

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifier-application)

Modifier Application


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#collection)

Collection

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined)
> 
> **👢📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.setmodifier-itemname-collection-scale)
> 
> _modifiers.setmodifier "ItemName" collection "scale"_
> 
> Where "ItemName" is the name of the item you want to manipulate,
> 
> and "scale" is the relative rate of collection for that particular item from collectables
> 
> (like hemp plants, nodettes, etc) (max 3).

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#example)

Example

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-1)
> 
> **👢📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.setmodifier-stones-collection-3)
> 
> _modifiers.setmodifier "Stones" collection "3"_
> 
> Players will collect 3x as much Stone as normal from Stone Nodettes.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#cook-amount)

Cook Amount

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-2)
> 
> **👢📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.setmodifier-itemname-cookamount-scale)
> 
> _modifiers.setmodifier "ItemName" cookamount "scale"_
> 
> Where "ItemName" is the name of the item you want to manipulate,
> 
> and "scale" is the relative yield received for that particular item when processed in a furnace.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#example-1)

Example

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-3)
> 
> **👢📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.setmodifier-metal.refined-cookamount-3)
> 
> _modifiers.setmodifier "metal.refined" cookamount "3"_
> 
> Triples yield when smelting HQM in a furnace.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#cook-speed)

Cook Speed

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-4)
> 
> **👢📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.setmodifier-itemname-cookspeed-scale)
> 
> _modifiers.setmodifier "ItemName" cookspeed "scale"_
> 
> Where "ItemName" is the name of the item you want to manipulate,
> 
> and "scale" is the relative speed at which that item will be processed by a furnace.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#example-2)

Example

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-5)
> 
> **👢📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.setmodifier-metal.ore-cookspeed-3)
> 
> _modifiers.setmodifier "metal.ore" cookspeed "3"_
> 
> Triples (3x) the cook speed of Metal Ore, effectively reducing the time taken to produce to a ⅓ of the base rate.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#crafting-speed)

> _modifiers.setmodifier "ItemName" craftspeed "scale"_
> 
> Where "ItemName" is the name of the item you want to manipulate,
> 
> and "scale" is a scale of how fast that particular item will take to craft.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#example-3)

> 
> Doubles the crafting speed when crafting a Tool Cupboard.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#crafting-time)

Crafting Time

> ###

> **👢📟**

> 
> _modifiers.setmodifier "ItemName" crafttime "value"_
> 
> Where "ItemName" is the name of the item you want to manipulate.
> 
> "Value" will override

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#example-4)

Example

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-9)
>

>

> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.setmodifier-cupboard.tool-crafttime-10)
> 
> _modifiers.setmodifier "cupboard.tool" crafttime "10"_
> 
> Overrides crafting time for crafting a Tool Cupboard and sets it to 10 seconds.

* * *

###

> _modifiers.setmodifier "ItemName" gather "scale"_
> 
> Where "ItemName" is the name of the item you want to manipulate,
> 
> and "scale" is the relative gathering rate for that particular item.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#example-5)

> 
> Players will collect twice as much Wood when harvesting directly from trees.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#tools)

Tools

> Where "ToolName" is the name of the tool you want to manipulate,

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#example-7)

Example

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-15)

> 
> Doubles gather rate on Hatchets. (Twice as many resources collected **per-hit**)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#workbench-level)

Workbench Level

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-16)
> 
> **👢📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.setmodifier-itemname-workbenchlevel-value)
> 
> _modifiers.setmodifier "ItemName" workbenchlevel "value"_
> 
> Where "ItemName" is the name of the item you want to manipulate,
> 
> and "value" sets the workbench tier required to craft the specified item.

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#example-8)

Example

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-17)
> 
> **👢📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.setmodifier-rifle.ak-workbenchlevel-1)
> 
> _modifiers.setmodifier "rifle.ak" workbenchlevel "1"_
> 
> Sets the Assault Rifle to be craftable with a Lvl 1 Workbench. You must still have the blueprint unlocked, and this does not unlock the Assault Rifle blueprint on the Tech Tree.

> 
> Where "scale" controls the relative speed of furnace cooking.
> 
> (Max 3)

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#example-9)

> ###

> 
> _craft.itemcookspeedmultiplier “2”_
> 
> Furnaces will cook twice as fast.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#furnace-efficiency)

> _craft.furnaceusagemultiplier “scale"_
> 
> Where "scale" controls the relative amount of Low Grade Fuel that furnaces use.
> 
> (Max 3)

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#example-10)

> 
> _craft.furnaceusagemultiplier “3"_
> 
> Furnaces will burn 3 times as much fuel when this is active.

✨NEW✨ Other Modifiers

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#charcoal-production)

Charcoal Production

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-24)

>

> _modifiers.charcoalratescale "scale"_
> 
> Where "scale" controls the relative amount of charcoal produced as a by-product of smelting and using furnaces. (Max 3)

> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-25)
> 
> **👢📟**
>

> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.charcoalratescale-3)

> _modifiers.charcoalratescale "3"_
> 
> Furnaces will produces triple the charcoal when smelting.

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#quarry-production)

Quarry Production

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-26)
> 
> **👢📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.quarryprocessratescale-scale)
> 
> _modifiers.quarryprocessratescale "scale"_
> 
> Where "scale" controls the relative speed of Ore/HQM/Stone production by a quarry. Works on all quarries. (Max 3)

**Example**

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-27)
> 
> **👢📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.quarryprocessratescale-3)
> 
> _modifiers.quarryprocessratescale "3"_
> 
> Quarries will produce the same amount of product, 3 times faster.

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#crude-oil-efficiency)

Low Grade Fuel Efficiency

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifier-management)

Modifier Management


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-32)
> 
> **👢📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.listmodifiers-itemname)
> 
> _modifiers.listmodifiers "ItemName"_
> 
> Outputs all of the currently active modifiers for a defined item, into the console.

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-33)
> 
> **👢📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.listallmodifiers)
> 
> _modifiers.listallmodifiers_
> 
> Outputs all the items that have modifiers, and their modifiers, into the console.

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-34)
> 
> **👢📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.clearmodifier-itemname-modifier)
> 
> _modifiers.clearmodifier "ItemName" "modifier"_
> 
> Removes a previously applied modifier from an item.
> 
> You can also use `"all"` to remove all of the modifiers on that item.

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#undefined-35)
> 
> **👢📟**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifiers.clearmodifiers)
> 
> _modifiers.clearmodifiers_
> 
> Removes all modifiers from all items.

*   [Quarry Production](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#quarry-production)
    
*   [Crude Oil Efficiency](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#crude-oil-efficiency)
    
*   [Low Grade Fuel Efficiency](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#low-grade-fuel-efficiency)
    
*   [Modifier Management](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/modifiers#modifier-management)
    

Was this helpful?

# AntiHack | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/moderation/antihack#server-owner)

Server Owner


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The table below contains a list of **AntiHack Commands** available for **Server Owners**.

Type

Command

Input

Description

Default

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/moderation/antihack#undefined-10)

**📟**

antihack.admincheat

`"0/1"`

Defines whether the AntiHack ignores noclip when used by Admins.

`1`

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/moderation/antihack#undefined)

**📟**

antihack.build\_losradius

`"number"`

Radius to check for deployables (Except sleeping bags/beds) when clipping into rocks/geometry.

`0.01`

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/moderation/antihack#undefined-1)

**📟**

antihack.build\_losradius\_sleepingbag

`"number"`

Radius to check for sleeping bags/beds when clipping into rocks/geometry.

`0.3`

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/moderation/antihack#undefined-2)

**📟**

antihack.build\_terraincheck

`"0/1"`

Toggles checking for terrain when placing deployables.

`1`

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/moderation/antihack#undefined-3)

**📟**

antihack.enforcementlevel

`"number"`

Toggles enforcement level for AntiHack violations. 0 = No enforcement 1 = Kick on violation

`1`

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/moderation/antihack#undefined-4)

**📟**

antihack.flyhack\_protection

`"number"`

Level of protection against flying players. 0 = disabled 1 = client 2 = capsule 3 = curve

`3`

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/moderation/antihack#undefined-5)

**📟**

antihack.melee\_protection

`"number"`

Level of protection to verify melee attacks. 0 = disabled 1 = initiator 2 = initiator + target 3 = initiator + target + LOS 4 = initiator + target + LOS + tickhistory

`4`

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/moderation/antihack#undefined-6)

**📟**

antihack.noclip\_protection

`"number"`

Level of protection against players clipping through objects. 0 = disabled 1 = ray 2 = sphere 3 = curve 4 = curve + alternative path

`4`

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/moderation/antihack#undefined-7)

**📟**

antihack.projectile\_protection

`"number"`

Level of protection to verify fired projectiles 0 = disabled 1 = speed 2 = speed + entity 3 = speed + entity + LOS 4 = speed + entity + LOS + trajectory 5 = speed + entity + LOS + trajectory + update 6 = speed + entity + LOS + trajectory + tickhistory

`6`

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/moderation/antihack#undefined-8)

**📟**

antihack.speedhack\_protection

`"number"`

Level of protection against players moving too quickly. 0 = disabled 1 = simple 2 = advanced

`0`

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/moderation/antihack#undefined-9)

**📟**

antihack.terrain\_check\_geometry

`"0/1"`

Toggles whether the player should be killed when inside world geometry. Occasionally has false positives inside certain monuments.

`0`

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/commands/moderation/antihack#server-admin)

# Kit Management | Rust Console Edition: Community Servers

Kits are customisable inventories that the player can spawn with if the Admin/Owner wishes.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kits-ui)

Kits UI


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We have implemented a new UI for buying, selling, and distributing kits to players on your community server.

This means that you no longer have to use commands in the GPORTAL | NITRADO console, but you can still use these commands if you wish.

circle-info

Be aware, there may be issues or conflicts if you are using both the commands **and** the UI at the same time.

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#starting-out)

Starting Out

From any point in the game, you can now open the Control Panel, and access the new Kit Manager.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FRLQqZ5rhDubbCmT12REV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def283241-827d-487e-9f02-0c8356f14d97&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c483157b&sv=2)

From here, you will be presented with a UI that looks like this:

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252Fu6MHkyr6M8G1B9LTaCaw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8ff98500-dbdf-424d-8a16-c87e86a498ad&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c573fac4&sv=2)

Selecting \[ADD KIT\] will present the player with a template player inventory. From here, the owner can add items, weapons, and clothing in any permutation they want.

Selecting a tile on the inventory will open the standard item list on the right side, allowing the owner to add appropriate items for that slot.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FeMVurwPrbmzGXS9KakLh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a48249d-4344-4f57-a6a3-30bba866a7de&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30b812ed&sv=2)

Here, you can select items, and they will be placed in the slot you selected.

circle-info

Be aware that only appropriate items can be placed in each of the inventory areas:

*   Clothing/Armour - Gear
    
*   All Items - Inventory
    
*   All Items - Belt
    

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252F5eM4D3BNz5hXSrOKmsgy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D284fdadc-0eae-4419-aba2-d56e6d8c0914&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cce34ba0&sv=2)

Once you have created your kit by placing items, you can edit its characteristics in the next panel. You have the option of changing:

*   Name
    
*   Description
    
*   Icon
    
*   Auth Level
    
    *   Users | VIPs | Mods | Admins | Owners
        
    
*   Visibility
    
    *   All
        
        *   This means all players can view this kit, but not necessarily buy/use it.
            
        
    *   Restricted
        
        *   Determines whether the kit is viewable for everyone, or restricted to the auth level listed above.
            
        
    

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252F89iQQfOLIfsRnOOUV341%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D440a5abb-2c75-47ef-a501-1a9e27a7eb02&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f14829b9&sv=2)

Your newly-created kit will appear in the UI as such:

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FpI18jOEC5BPg6kqhk8cm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De17621b2-1442-4107-a8dc-012705c2b902&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e0ceca7a&sv=2)

From here, you can further manipulate your created kit.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FAWwrYGiTrm3CKlMNGqbF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6bc68174-e7e6-47f2-ae9d-9f8a31db583a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9b73dd12&sv=2)

You have the following options:

*   Modify Kit
    
    *   This will take you back to the kit creation screen where you can edit and add items
        
    
*   View Details
    
    *   Here you can view additional information about the kit.
        
    
*   Give Kit to Player
    
    *   You can choose a player on the server to grant a kit to for one-time use.
        
    
*   Give Kit to Auth Level Group
    
    *   Same as above, but for entire auth levels.
        
    
*   Put Kit in the Vendor
    
    *   You can add/remove up to 7 kits to the Kit Vending Machine, so that people may buy them with in-game items.
        
    
*   Delete kit
    
    *   This will delete the kit from the UI completely.
        
    

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-vending)

Kit Vending


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Kit Vending Machine \[KVM\] is a special type of Vending Machine that Owners/Admins can place around the map to sell created kits to players in the server.

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FjTQ4NVO5Qr0gEv8lns6Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3eda6eaa-1e54-4d08-af95-de2674af0827&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=55ed9fe3&sv=2)

circle-info

You can spawn a Kits Machine from the Item Spawn menu. (Admin+ only)

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#using-the-kvm-seller)

Using the KVM - Seller

To place kits in the Kit Vending Machine, you must first create a kit using the guide above.

After a kit has been created, go to the kit in the UI and select \[Put Kit in Vendor\].

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FdgeqYuJef34nRH6KIpXg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D42d77d83-ab7b-4d70-93cb-f1873d8f6e3c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=58d840f&sv=2)

You have the following options to modify your kits for the KVM:

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#market-configuration)

Market Configuration

*   For Sale
    
    *   Enables/Disables the selling of the kit in a KVM.
        
    *   TRUE | FALSE
        
    
*   Kit Amount
    
    *   Defines the maximum amount of kits that can be stored in a KVM at any time.
        
    *   1 -> ∞
        
    
*   Kit Restock Amount
    
    *   Defines the amount of Kits restocked per tick (defined below).
        
    *   0 -> 9999
        
    
*   Kit Restock Time
    
    *   Defines the amount of time taken per restock. Lower is faster.
        
    *   1s -> 365d 23h 59m 59s
        
    
*   Acquisition Per Player
    
    *   Defines how many kits players are allowed to purchase at any one time.
        
    *   1 -> ∞
        
    
*   Acquisition Cooldown
    
    *   Defines the amount of time that must pass before the player is allowed to purchase this particular kit from the KVM again.
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-pricing)

Kit Pricing

*   Currency Amount
    
    *   Defines the amount of a certain item that is taken from the player in exchange for the kit.
        
    *   0 -> 9999
        
    
*   Currency Item
    
    *   Defines what kind of item the player must have in order to purchase the kit. This option opens the items list.
        
    *   Any item
        
    

![](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3429851128-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F989RjbRw8ybjBIxJvMra%252Fuploads%252FOHy7HpaZRySvnHabzLEW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df427c352-8e5a-4cd2-8493-e0e4ceb54c48&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e62bc0a3&sv=2)

A fully customised KVM setup.

After pressing the \[CONFIRM\] button, your kit should appear in all KVMs around the map instantly, and be available to purchase with the settings you chose earlier.

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#using-the-kvm-buyer)

Using the KVM - Buyer

Using the KVM is the same as interacting with a normal Vending Machine. Simply approach it, press the interact button shown on screen, and broswe the available kits.

You may encounter different scenarios, based on your Auth Level, affordability, or availability.

*   \[BUY\]
    
    *   This Kit is available to buy, and you can afford it.
        
    
*   \[CAN'T AFFORD\]
    
    *   This Kit is available to buy, but you can't afford it.
        
    
*   \[AUTH TIER ONLY\]
    
    *   This Kit is not available to you, as you do do not have the sufficient Auth Level to purchase it.
        
    

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#command-based-kit-creation)

Command-based Kit Creation


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use the following command to create a kit, containing the items of your choice:

circle-info

We have implemented a maximum limit of 128 kits per server.

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#undefined)
> 
> **📟🎮**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-add-0-1-2-3-4)
> 
> _**kit add \[0\] \[1\] \[2\] \[3\] \[4\]**_
> 
> This command adds an item to a kit, with the following 5 options:
> 
> (When you use this command for the first time, the kit will be created and you can add items to it by repeating the above command with different items)

#

Option

Input Type

Description

`[0]`

Kit Name

`"string"`

Defines the name of the Kit that you want to create. For names with spaces, you must surround the name in quotation marks.

`[1]`

Item Name

`"itemname"`

Defines the item that you would like to add. For a list of items, [_Corrosion hour's guide to Rust_arrow-up-right](https://www.corrosionhour.com/rust-item-list/)
 is a good resource.

`[2]`

Amount

`"number"`

Defines the amount of items that you would like to add. This adheres to current MaxStack rules on your server.

`[3]`

Condition

`"number"`

Defines the condition of the item you would like to add. This can range from `0-1`

`[4]`

Container

`"Main" | "Belt" | "Wear"`

Defines which inventory area you would like the item to be placed in.

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-information)

Kit Information


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#undefined-1)
> 
> **📟🎮**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-info-kitname)
> 
> _kit info "KitName"_
> 
> Returns useful info about the chosen kit and prints it into the log.

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#undefined-2)
> 
> **📟🎮**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-list)
> 
> _kit list_
> 
> Lists all active Kits in the server into the log.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-removal)

Kit Removal


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#undefined-3)
> 
> **📟🎮**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-remove-kitname-id)
> 
> _kit remove "KitName" "ID"_
> 
> Where "kitname" is the name of the kit you would like to manipulate,
> 
> and "ID" is the ID of the item you would like to remove.
> 
> You can find this ID by running the above command `kit info "KitName"`

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#undefined-4)
> 
> **📟🎮**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-delete-kitname)
> 
> kit delete "KitName"
> 
> Deletes all items in the chosen Kit, then delets the Kit.

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-name-changing)

Kit Name Changing


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can edit any active kits by using the following commands:

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#undefined-5)
> 
> **📟🎮**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-edit-kitname-changename-newname)
> 
> _kit edit "KitName" changename "NewName"_
> 
> Changes the old "KitName" to "NewName".

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-group-changing)

Kit Group Changing


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#undefined-6)
> 
> **📟🎮**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-edit-kitname-addgroup-group)
> 
> _kit edit "KitName" addgroup "Group"_
> 
> Adds the defined "kit" to spawn for all users in the defined "group".

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#undefined-7)
> 
> **📟🎮**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-edit-kitname-removegroup-group)
> 
> _kit edit "KitName" removegroup "Group"_
> 
> Removes the defined "kit" to spawn for all users in the defined "group".

The valid groups are:

*   User
    
*   VIP
    
*   Moderator
    
*   Admin
    
*   Owner
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-gifting)

Kit Gifting


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Admins can also gift a kit to a single player, group, or all players on the server.

circle-info

NOTE: This method of giving Kits will only give them a Kit once. They will be lost upon dying unless you have set up Kit groups (above).

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#group)

Group

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#undefined-8)
> 
> **📟🎮**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-givetogroup-kitname-group)
> 
> _kit givetogroup "kitname" "group"_
> 
> Where "kitname" is the name of the kit you would like to gift,
> 
> and "group" is any Auth Tier listed above.

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#player)

Player

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#undefined-9)
> 
> **📟🎮**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-givetoplayer-kitname-id)
> 
> _kit givetoplayer "kitname" "ID"_
> 
> Where "kitname" is the name of the kit you would like to gift,
> 
> and "ID" is the in-game name of the player you choose.

### 

[hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#all-players)

All Players

> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#undefined-10)
> 
> **📟🎮**
> 
> ### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://rust-console-edition.gitbook.io/community-servers/feature-guides/kit-management#kit-giveall-kitname)
> 
> _kit giveall "kitname"_
> 
> Where "kitname" is the name of the kit you would like to gift.

**📟**

global.banid

`"ID" "reason" "time"`

Bans the specified “user” from the current server indefinitely. Adding a reason will display that reason in the logs. Adding a time will ban the player for that amount of time, measured in seconds. Example: `banid "2stageFright" "2stageFright for: writing bad wiki pages" "600"` Would ban user "2StageFright" for writing bad wiki pages, and the ban would last 10 minutes,
